1861     initialize_hashtable(names_and_sigs);
1862     bool dup = false;
1863     const Symbol* name = NULL;
1864     const Symbol* sig = NULL;
1865     {
1866       debug_only(NoSafepointVerifier nsv;)
1867       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
1868         name = fs.name();
1869         sig = fs.signature();
1870         // If no duplicates, add name/signature in hashtable names_and_sigs.
1871         if (!put_after_lookup(name, sig, names_and_sigs)) {
1872           dup = true;
1873           break;
1874         }
1875       }
1876     }
1877     if (dup) {
1878       classfile_parse_error("Duplicate field name \"%s\" with signature \"%s\" in class file %s",
1879                              name->as_C_string(), sig->as_klass_external_name(), CHECK);
1880     }
1881   }
1882 }
1883 
1884 
1885 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_exception_table(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
1886                                                                          u4 code_length,
1887                                                                          u4 exception_table_length,
1888                                                                          TRAPS) {
1889   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
1890 
1891   const unsafe_u2* const exception_table_start = cfs->current();
1892   assert(exception_table_start != NULL, "null exception table");
1893 
1894   cfs->guarantee_more(8 * exception_table_length, CHECK_NULL); // start_pc,
1895                                                                // end_pc,
1896                                                                // handler_pc,
1897                                                                // catch_type_index
1898 
1899   // Will check legal target after parsing code array in verifier.
1900   if (_need_verify) {
1901     for (unsigned int i = 0; i < exception_table_length; i++) {
1902       const u2 start_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1903       const u2 end_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1904       const u2 handler_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1905       const u2 catch_type_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1906       guarantee_property((start_pc < end_pc) && (end_pc <= code_length),
1907                          "Illegal exception table range in class file %s",
1908                          CHECK_NULL);
1909       guarantee_property(handler_pc < code_length,
1910                          "Illegal exception table handler in class file %s",
1911                          CHECK_NULL);
1912       if (catch_type_index != 0) {
1913         guarantee_property(valid_klass_reference_at(catch_type_index),
1914                            "Catch type in exception table has bad constant type in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
1915       }
1916     }
1917   } else {
1918     cfs->skip_u2_fast(exception_table_length * 4);
1919   }
1920   return exception_table_start;
1921 }
1922 
1923 void ClassFileParser::parse_linenumber_table(u4 code_attribute_length,
1924                                              u4 code_length,
1925                                              CompressedLineNumberWriteStream**const write_stream,
1926                                              TRAPS) {
1927 
1928   const ClassFileStream* const cfs = _stream;
1929   unsigned int num_entries = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
1930 
1931   // Each entry is a u2 start_pc, and a u2 line_number
1932   const unsigned int length_in_bytes = num_entries * (sizeof(u2) * 2);
1933 
1934   // Verify line number attribute and table length
1935   check_property(
1936     code_attribute_length == sizeof(u2) + length_in_bytes,
1937     "LineNumberTable attribute has wrong length in class file %s", CHECK);
1938 
1939   cfs->guarantee_more(length_in_bytes, CHECK);
1940 
1941   if ((*write_stream) == NULL) {
1942     if (length_in_bytes > fixed_buffer_size) {
1943       (*write_stream) = new CompressedLineNumberWriteStream(length_in_bytes);
1944     } else {
1945       (*write_stream) = new CompressedLineNumberWriteStream(
1946         _linenumbertable_buffer, fixed_buffer_size);
1947     }
1948   }
1949 
1950   while (num_entries-- > 0) {
1951     const u2 bci  = cfs->get_u2_fast(); // start_pc
1952     const u2 line = cfs->get_u2_fast(); // line_number
1953     guarantee_property(bci < code_length,
1954         "Invalid pc in LineNumberTable in class file %s", CHECK);
1955     (*write_stream)->write_pair(bci, line);
1956   }
1957 }
1958 
1959 
1960 class LVT_Hash : public AllStatic {
1961  public:
1962 
1963   static bool equals(LocalVariableTableElement const& e0, LocalVariableTableElement const& e1) {
1964   /*
1965    * 3-tuple start_bci/length/slot has to be unique key,
1966    * so the following comparison seems to be redundant:
1967    *       && elem->name_cp_index == entry->_elem->name_cp_index
1968    */
1969     return (e0.start_bci     == e1.start_bci &&
1970             e0.length        == e1.length &&
1971             e0.name_cp_index == e1.name_cp_index &&
1972             e0.slot          == e1.slot);
1973   }
1974 
1975   static unsigned int hash(LocalVariableTableElement const& e0) {
1976     unsigned int raw_hash = e0.start_bci;
1977 
1978     raw_hash = e0.length        + raw_hash * 37;
1979     raw_hash = e0.name_cp_index + raw_hash * 37;
1980     raw_hash = e0.slot          + raw_hash * 37;
1981 
1982     return raw_hash;
1983   }
1984 };
1985 
1986 
1987 // Class file LocalVariableTable elements.
1988 class Classfile_LVT_Element {
1989  public:
1990   u2 start_bci;
1991   u2 length;
1992   u2 name_cp_index;
1993   u2 descriptor_cp_index;
1994   u2 slot;
1995 };
1996 
1997 static void copy_lvt_element(const Classfile_LVT_Element* const src,
1998                              LocalVariableTableElement* const lvt) {
1999   lvt->start_bci           = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->start_bci);
2000   lvt->length              = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->length);
2001   lvt->name_cp_index       = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->name_cp_index);
2002   lvt->descriptor_cp_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->descriptor_cp_index);
2003   lvt->signature_cp_index  = 0;
2004   lvt->slot                = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->slot);
2005 }
2006 
2007 // Function is used to parse both attributes:
2008 // LocalVariableTable (LVT) and LocalVariableTypeTable (LVTT)
2009 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_localvariable_table(const ClassFileStream* cfs,
2010                                                                              u4 code_length,
2011                                                                              u2 max_locals,
2012                                                                              u4 code_attribute_length,
2013                                                                              u2* const localvariable_table_length,
2014                                                                              bool isLVTT,
2015                                                                              TRAPS) {
2016   const char* const tbl_name = (isLVTT) ? "LocalVariableTypeTable" : "LocalVariableTable";
2017   *localvariable_table_length = cfs->get_u2(CHECK_NULL);
2018   const unsigned int size =
2019     (*localvariable_table_length) * sizeof(Classfile_LVT_Element) / sizeof(u2);
2020 
2021   const ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
2022 
2023   // Verify local variable table attribute has right length
2024   if (_need_verify) {
2025     guarantee_property(code_attribute_length == (sizeof(*localvariable_table_length) + size * sizeof(u2)),
2026                        "%s has wrong length in class file %s", tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2027   }
2028 
2029   const unsafe_u2* const localvariable_table_start = cfs->current();
2030   assert(localvariable_table_start != NULL, "null local variable table");
2031   if (!_need_verify) {
2032     cfs->skip_u2_fast(size);
2033   } else {
2034     cfs->guarantee_more(size * 2, CHECK_NULL);
2035     for(int i = 0; i < (*localvariable_table_length); i++) {
2036       const u2 start_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2037       const u2 length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2038       const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2039       const u2 descriptor_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2040       const u2 index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2041       // Assign to a u4 to avoid overflow
2042       const u4 end_pc = (u4)start_pc + (u4)length;
2043 
2044       if (start_pc >= code_length) {
2045         classfile_parse_error(
2046           "Invalid start_pc %u in %s in class file %s",
2047           start_pc, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2048       }
2049       if (end_pc > code_length) {
2050         classfile_parse_error(
2051           "Invalid length %u in %s in class file %s",
2052           length, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2053       }
2054       const int cp_size = cp->length();
2055       guarantee_property(valid_symbol_at(name_index),
2056         "Name index %u in %s has bad constant type in class file %s",
2057         name_index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2058       guarantee_property(valid_symbol_at(descriptor_index),
2059         "Signature index %u in %s has bad constant type in class file %s",
2060         descriptor_index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2061 
2062       const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
2063       const Symbol* const sig = cp->symbol_at(descriptor_index);
2064       verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK_NULL);
2065       u2 extra_slot = 0;
2066       if (!isLVTT) {
2067         verify_legal_field_signature(name, sig, CHECK_NULL);
2068 
2069         // 4894874: check special cases for double and long local variables
2070         if (sig == vmSymbols::type_signature(T_DOUBLE) ||
2071             sig == vmSymbols::type_signature(T_LONG)) {
2072           extra_slot = 1;
2073         }
2074       }
2075       guarantee_property((index + extra_slot) < max_locals,
2076                           "Invalid index %u in %s in class file %s",
2077                           index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2078     }
2079   }
2080   return localvariable_table_start;
2081 }
2082 
2083 static const u1* parse_stackmap_table(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2084                                       u4 code_attribute_length,
2085                                       bool need_verify,
2086                                       TRAPS) {
2087   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2088 
2089   if (0 == code_attribute_length) {
2090     return NULL;
2091   }
2092 
2093   const u1* const stackmap_table_start = cfs->current();
2094   assert(stackmap_table_start != NULL, "null stackmap table");
2095 
2096   // check code_attribute_length first
2097   cfs->skip_u1(code_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2098 
2099   if (!need_verify && !DumpSharedSpaces) {
2100     return NULL;
2101   }
2102   return stackmap_table_start;
2103 }
2104 
2105 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_checked_exceptions(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2106                                                                             u2* const checked_exceptions_length,
2107                                                                             u4 method_attribute_length,
2108                                                                             TRAPS) {
2109   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2110   assert(checked_exceptions_length != NULL, "invariant");
2111 
2112   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // checked_exceptions_length
2113   *checked_exceptions_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2114   const unsigned int size =
2115     (*checked_exceptions_length) * sizeof(CheckedExceptionElement) / sizeof(u2);
2116   const unsafe_u2* const checked_exceptions_start = cfs->current();
2117   assert(checked_exceptions_start != NULL, "null checked exceptions");
2118   if (!_need_verify) {
2119     cfs->skip_u2_fast(size);
2120   } else {
2121     // Verify each value in the checked exception table
2122     u2 checked_exception;
2123     const u2 len = *checked_exceptions_length;
2124     cfs->guarantee_more(2 * len, CHECK_NULL);
2125     for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
2126       checked_exception = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2127       check_property(
2128         valid_klass_reference_at(checked_exception),
2129         "Exception name has bad type at constant pool %u in class file %s",
2130         checked_exception, CHECK_NULL);
2131     }
2132   }
2133   // check exceptions attribute length
2134   if (_need_verify) {
2135     guarantee_property(method_attribute_length == (sizeof(*checked_exceptions_length) +
2136                                                    sizeof(u2) * size),
2137                       "Exceptions attribute has wrong length in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2138   }
2139   return checked_exceptions_start;
2140 }
2141 
2142 void ClassFileParser::throwIllegalSignature(const char* type,
2143                                             const Symbol* name,
2144                                             const Symbol* sig,
2145                                             TRAPS) const {
2146   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
2147   assert(sig != NULL, "invariant");
2148 
2149   const char* class_note = "";
2150   if (is_inline_type() && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
2151     class_note = " (an inline class)";
2152   }
2153 
2154   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2155   Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
2156       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
2157       "%s \"%s\" in class %s%s has illegal signature \"%s\"", type,
2158       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, sig->as_C_string());
2159 }
2160 
2161 AnnotationCollector::ID
2162 AnnotationCollector::annotation_index(const ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
2163                                       const Symbol* name,
2164                                       const bool can_access_vm_annotations) {
2165   const vmSymbols::SID sid = vmSymbols::find_sid(name);
2166   // Privileged code can use all annotations.  Other code silently drops some.
2167   const bool privileged = loader_data->is_boot_class_loader_data() ||
2168                           loader_data->is_platform_class_loader_data() ||
2169                           can_access_vm_annotations;
2170   switch (sid) {
2171     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(reflect_CallerSensitive_signature): {
2172       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2173       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2174       return _method_CallerSensitive;
2175     }
2176     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ForceInline_signature): {
2177       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2178       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2179       return _method_ForceInline;
2180     }
2181     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_DontInline_signature): {
2182       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2183       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2184       return _method_DontInline;
2185     }
2186     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(java_lang_invoke_InjectedProfile_signature): {
2187       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2188       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2189       return _method_InjectedProfile;
2190     }
2191     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(java_lang_invoke_LambdaForm_Compiled_signature): {
2192       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2193       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2194       return _method_LambdaForm_Compiled;
2195     }
2196     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Hidden_signature): {
2197       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2198       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2199       return _method_Hidden;
2200     }
2201     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate_signature): {
2202       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2203       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2204       return _method_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate;
2205     }
2206     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Stable_signature): {
2207       if (_location != _in_field)   break;  // only allow for fields
2208       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2209       return _field_Stable;
2210     }
2211     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended_signature): {
2212       if (_location != _in_field && _location != _in_class) {
2213         break;  // only allow for fields and classes
2214       }
2215       if (!EnableContended || (RestrictContended && !privileged)) {
2216         break;  // honor privileges
2217       }
2218       return _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended;
2219     }
2220     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess_signature): {
2221       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2222       if (RestrictReservedStack && !privileged) break; // honor privileges
2223       return _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess;
2224     }
2225     default: {
2226       break;
2227     }
2228   }
2229   return AnnotationCollector::_unknown;
2230 }
2231 
2232 void ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector::apply_to(FieldInfo* f) {
2233   if (is_contended())
2234     f->set_contended_group(contended_group());
2235   if (is_stable())
2236     f->set_stable(true);
2237 }
2238 
2239 ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector::~FieldAnnotationCollector() {
2240   // If there's an error deallocate metadata for field annotations
2241   MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _field_annotations);
2242   MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _field_type_annotations);
2243 }
2244 
2245 void MethodAnnotationCollector::apply_to(const methodHandle& m) {
2246   if (has_annotation(_method_CallerSensitive))
2247     m->set_caller_sensitive(true);
2248   if (has_annotation(_method_ForceInline))
2249     m->set_force_inline(true);
2250   if (has_annotation(_method_DontInline))
2251     m->set_dont_inline(true);
2252   if (has_annotation(_method_InjectedProfile))
2253     m->set_has_injected_profile(true);
2254   if (has_annotation(_method_LambdaForm_Compiled) && m->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none)
2255     m->set_intrinsic_id(vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm);
2256   if (has_annotation(_method_Hidden))
2257     m->set_hidden(true);
2258   if (has_annotation(_method_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate) && !m->is_synthetic())
2259     m->set_intrinsic_candidate(true);
2260   if (has_annotation(_jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess))
2261     m->set_has_reserved_stack_access(true);
2262 }
2263 
2264 void ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector::apply_to(InstanceKlass* ik) {
2265   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
2266   ik->set_is_contended(is_contended());
2267 }
2268 
2269 #define MAX_ARGS_SIZE 255
2270 #define MAX_CODE_SIZE 65535
2271 #define INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER 256
2272 
2273 /* Copy class file LVT's/LVTT's into the HotSpot internal LVT.
2274  *
2275  * Rules for LVT's and LVTT's are:
2276  *   - There can be any number of LVT's and LVTT's.
2277  *   - If there are n LVT's, it is the same as if there was just
2278  *     one LVT containing all the entries from the n LVT's.
2279  *   - There may be no more than one LVT entry per local variable.
2280  *     Two LVT entries are 'equal' if these fields are the same:
2281  *        start_pc, length, name, slot
2282  *   - There may be no more than one LVTT entry per each LVT entry.
2283  *     Each LVTT entry has to match some LVT entry.
2284  *   - HotSpot internal LVT keeps natural ordering of class file LVT entries.
2285  */
2286 void ClassFileParser::copy_localvariable_table(const ConstMethod* cm,
2287                                                int lvt_cnt,
2288                                                u2* const localvariable_table_length,
2289                                                const unsafe_u2** const localvariable_table_start,
2290                                                int lvtt_cnt,
2291                                                u2* const localvariable_type_table_length,
2292                                                const unsafe_u2** const localvariable_type_table_start,
2293                                                TRAPS) {
2294 
2295   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2296 
2297   typedef ResourceHashtable<LocalVariableTableElement, LocalVariableTableElement*,
2298                             &LVT_Hash::hash, &LVT_Hash::equals> LVT_HashTable;
2299 
2300   LVT_HashTable* const table = new LVT_HashTable();
2301 
2302   // To fill LocalVariableTable in
2303   const Classfile_LVT_Element* cf_lvt;
2304   LocalVariableTableElement* lvt = cm->localvariable_table_start();
2305 
2306   for (int tbl_no = 0; tbl_no < lvt_cnt; tbl_no++) {
2307     cf_lvt = (Classfile_LVT_Element *) localvariable_table_start[tbl_no];
2308     for (int idx = 0; idx < localvariable_table_length[tbl_no]; idx++, lvt++) {
2309       copy_lvt_element(&cf_lvt[idx], lvt);
2310       // If no duplicates, add LVT elem in hashtable.
2311       if (table->put(*lvt, lvt) == false
2312           && _need_verify
2313           && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
2314         classfile_parse_error("Duplicated LocalVariableTable attribute "
2315                               "entry for '%s' in class file %s",
2316                                _cp->symbol_at(lvt->name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2317                                CHECK);
2318       }
2319     }
2320   }
2321 
2322   // To merge LocalVariableTable and LocalVariableTypeTable
2323   const Classfile_LVT_Element* cf_lvtt;
2324   LocalVariableTableElement lvtt_elem;
2325 
2326   for (int tbl_no = 0; tbl_no < lvtt_cnt; tbl_no++) {
2327     cf_lvtt = (Classfile_LVT_Element *) localvariable_type_table_start[tbl_no];
2328     for (int idx = 0; idx < localvariable_type_table_length[tbl_no]; idx++) {
2329       copy_lvt_element(&cf_lvtt[idx], &lvtt_elem);
2330       LocalVariableTableElement** entry = table->get(lvtt_elem);
2331       if (entry == NULL) {
2332         if (_need_verify) {
2333           classfile_parse_error("LVTT entry for '%s' in class file %s "
2334                                 "does not match any LVT entry",
2335                                  _cp->symbol_at(lvtt_elem.name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2336                                  CHECK);
2337         }
2338       } else if ((*entry)->signature_cp_index != 0 && _need_verify) {
2339         classfile_parse_error("Duplicated LocalVariableTypeTable attribute "
2340                               "entry for '%s' in class file %s",
2341                                _cp->symbol_at(lvtt_elem.name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2342                                CHECK);
2343       } else {
2344         // to add generic signatures into LocalVariableTable
2345         (*entry)->signature_cp_index = lvtt_elem.descriptor_cp_index;
2346       }
2347     }
2348   }
2349 }
2350 
2351 
2352 void ClassFileParser::copy_method_annotations(ConstMethod* cm,
2353                                        const u1* runtime_visible_annotations,
2354                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2355                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations,
2356                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2357                                        const u1* runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
2358                                        int runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
2359                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
2360                                        int runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2361                                        const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations,
2362                                        int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
2363                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
2364                                        int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2365                                        const u1* annotation_default,
2366                                        int annotation_default_length,
2367                                        TRAPS) {
2368 
2369   AnnotationArray* a;
2370 
2371   if (runtime_visible_annotations_length +
2372       runtime_invisible_annotations_length > 0) {
2373      a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
2374                               runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2375                               runtime_invisible_annotations,
2376                               runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2377                               CHECK);
2378      cm->set_method_annotations(a);
2379   }
2380 
2381   if (runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length +
2382       runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length > 0) {
2383     a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
2384                              runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
2385                              runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
2386                              runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2387                              CHECK);
2388     cm->set_parameter_annotations(a);
2389   }
2390 
2391   if (annotation_default_length > 0) {
2392     a = assemble_annotations(annotation_default,
2393                              annotation_default_length,
2394                              NULL,
2395                              0,
2396                              CHECK);
2397     cm->set_default_annotations(a);
2398   }
2399 
2400   if (runtime_visible_type_annotations_length +
2401       runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length > 0) {
2402     a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
2403                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
2404                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
2405                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2406                              CHECK);
2407     cm->set_type_annotations(a);
2408   }
2409 }
2410 
2411 
2412 // Note: the parse_method below is big and clunky because all parsing of the code and exceptions
2413 // attribute is inlined. This is cumbersome to avoid since we inline most of the parts in the
2414 // Method* to save footprint, so we only know the size of the resulting Method* when the
2415 // entire method attribute is parsed.
2416 //
2417 // The promoted_flags parameter is used to pass relevant access_flags
2418 // from the method back up to the containing klass. These flag values
2419 // are added to klass's access_flags.
2420 
2421 Method* ClassFileParser::parse_method(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2422                                       bool is_interface,
2423                                       bool is_inline_type,
2424                                       const ConstantPool* cp,
2425                                       AccessFlags* const promoted_flags,
2426                                       TRAPS) {
2427   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2428   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
2429   assert(promoted_flags != NULL, "invariant");
2430 
2431   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2432   // Parse fixed parts:
2433   // access_flags, name_index, descriptor_index, attributes_count
2434   cfs->guarantee_more(8, CHECK_NULL);
2435 
2436   int flags = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2437   const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2438   const int cp_size = cp->length();
2439   check_property(
2440     valid_symbol_at(name_index),
2441     "Illegal constant pool index %u for method name in class file %s",
2442     name_index, CHECK_NULL);
2443   const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
2444   verify_legal_method_name(name, CHECK_NULL);
2445 
2446   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2447   guarantee_property(
2448     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
2449     "Illegal constant pool index %u for method signature in class file %s",
2450     signature_index, CHECK_NULL);
2451   const Symbol* const signature = cp->symbol_at(signature_index);
2452 
2453   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
2454     // We ignore the other access flags for a valid class initializer.
2455     // (JVM Spec 2nd ed., chapter 4.6)
2456     if (_major_version < 51) { // backward compatibility
2457       flags = JVM_ACC_STATIC;
2458     } else if ((flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC) == JVM_ACC_STATIC) {
2459       flags &= JVM_ACC_STATIC | JVM_ACC_STRICT;
2460     } else {
2461       classfile_parse_error("Method <clinit> is not static in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2462     }
2463   } else {
2464     verify_legal_method_modifiers(flags, is_interface, is_inline_type, name, CHECK_NULL);
2465   }
2466 
2467   if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
2468     if (is_interface) {
2469       classfile_parse_error("Interface cannot have a method named <init>, class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2470     } else if (!is_inline_type && signature->is_void_method_signature()) {
2471       // OK, a constructor
2472     } else if (is_inline_type && !signature->is_void_method_signature()) {
2473       // also OK, a static factory, as long as the return value is good
2474       bool ok = false;
2475       SignatureStream ss((Symbol*) signature, true);
2476       while (!ss.at_return_type())  ss.next();
2477       if (ss.is_reference()) {
2478         Symbol* ret = ss.as_symbol();
2479         const Symbol* required = class_name();
2480         if (is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
2481           // The original class name in the UAC byte stream gets changed.  So
2482           // using the original name in the return type is no longer valid.
2483           required = vmSymbols::java_lang_Object();
2484         }
2485         ok = (ret == required);
2486       }
2487       if (!ok) {
2488         throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
2489       }
2490     } else {
2491       // not OK, so throw the same error as in verify_legal_method_signature.
2492       throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
2493     }
2494     // A declared <init> method must always be either a non-static
2495     // object constructor, with a void return, or else it must be a
2496     // static factory method, with a non-void return.  No other
2497     // definition of <init> is possible.
2498     //
2499     // The verifier (in verify_invoke_instructions) will inspect the
2500     // signature of any attempt to invoke <init>, and ensures that it
2501     // returns non-void if and only if it is being invoked by
2502     // invokestatic, and void if and only if it is being invoked by
2503     // invokespecial.
2504     //
2505     // When a symbolic reference to <init> is resolved for a
2506     // particular invocation mode (special or static), the mode is
2507     // matched to the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier of the <init> method.
2508     // Thus, it is impossible to statically invoke a constructor, and
2509     // impossible to "new + invokespecial" a static factory, either
2510     // through bytecode or through reflection.
2511   }
2512 
2513   int args_size = -1;  // only used when _need_verify is true
2514   if (_need_verify) {
2515     args_size = ((flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC) ? 0 : 1) +
2516                  verify_legal_method_signature(name, signature, CHECK_NULL);
2517     if (args_size > MAX_ARGS_SIZE) {
2518       classfile_parse_error("Too many arguments in method signature in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2519     }
2520   }
2521 
2522   AccessFlags access_flags(flags & JVM_RECOGNIZED_METHOD_MODIFIERS);
2523 
2524   // Default values for code and exceptions attribute elements
2525   u2 max_stack = 0;
2526   u2 max_locals = 0;
2527   u4 code_length = 0;
2528   const u1* code_start = 0;
2529   u2 exception_table_length = 0;
2530   const unsafe_u2* exception_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of u2 elements
2531   Array<int>* exception_handlers = Universe::the_empty_int_array();
2532   u2 checked_exceptions_length = 0;
2533   const unsafe_u2* checked_exceptions_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of u2 elements
2534   CompressedLineNumberWriteStream* linenumber_table = NULL;
2535   int linenumber_table_length = 0;
2536   int total_lvt_length = 0;
2537   u2 lvt_cnt = 0;
2538   u2 lvtt_cnt = 0;
2539   bool lvt_allocated = false;
2540   u2 max_lvt_cnt = INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER;
2541   u2 max_lvtt_cnt = INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER;
2542   u2* localvariable_table_length = NULL;
2543   const unsafe_u2** localvariable_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of LVT attributes
2544   u2* localvariable_type_table_length = NULL;
2545   const unsafe_u2** localvariable_type_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to LVTT attributes
2546   int method_parameters_length = -1;
2547   const u1* method_parameters_data = NULL;
2548   bool method_parameters_seen = false;
2549   bool parsed_code_attribute = false;
2550   bool parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute = false;
2551   bool parsed_stackmap_attribute = false;
2552   // stackmap attribute - JDK1.5
2553   const u1* stackmap_data = NULL;
2554   int stackmap_data_length = 0;
2555   u2 generic_signature_index = 0;
2556   MethodAnnotationCollector parsed_annotations;
2557   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
2558   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
2559   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
2560   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
2561   const u1* runtime_visible_parameter_annotations = NULL;
2562   int runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length = 0;
2563   const u1* runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations = NULL;
2564   int runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length = 0;
2565   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
2566   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
2567   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
2568   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
2569   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
2570   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
2571   bool runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists = false;
2572   const u1* annotation_default = NULL;
2573   int annotation_default_length = 0;
2574 
2575   // Parse code and exceptions attribute
2576   u2 method_attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2577   while (method_attributes_count--) {
2578     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_NULL);  // method_attribute_name_index, method_attribute_length
2579     const u2 method_attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2580     const u4 method_attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2581     check_property(
2582       valid_symbol_at(method_attribute_name_index),
2583       "Invalid method attribute name index %u in class file %s",
2584       method_attribute_name_index, CHECK_NULL);
2585 
2586     const Symbol* const method_attribute_name = cp->symbol_at(method_attribute_name_index);
2587     if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_code()) {
2588       // Parse Code attribute
2589       if (_need_verify) {
2590         guarantee_property(
2591             !access_flags.is_native() && !access_flags.is_abstract(),
2592                         "Code attribute in native or abstract methods in class file %s",
2593                          CHECK_NULL);
2594       }
2595       if (parsed_code_attribute) {
2596         classfile_parse_error("Multiple Code attributes in class file %s",
2597                               CHECK_NULL);
2598       }
2599       parsed_code_attribute = true;
2600 
2601       // Stack size, locals size, and code size
2602       cfs->guarantee_more(8, CHECK_NULL);
2603       max_stack = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2604       max_locals = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2605       code_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2606       if (_need_verify) {
2607         guarantee_property(args_size <= max_locals,
2608                            "Arguments can't fit into locals in class file %s",
2609                            CHECK_NULL);
2610         guarantee_property(code_length > 0 && code_length <= MAX_CODE_SIZE,
2611                            "Invalid method Code length %u in class file %s",
2612                            code_length, CHECK_NULL);
2613       }
2614       // Code pointer
2615       code_start = cfs->current();
2616       assert(code_start != NULL, "null code start");
2617       cfs->guarantee_more(code_length, CHECK_NULL);
2618       cfs->skip_u1_fast(code_length);
2619 
2620       // Exception handler table
2621       cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // exception_table_length
2622       exception_table_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2623       if (exception_table_length > 0) {
2624         exception_table_start = parse_exception_table(cfs,
2625                                                       code_length,
2626                                                       exception_table_length,
2627                                                       CHECK_NULL);
2628       }
2629 
2630       // Parse additional attributes in code attribute
2631       cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // code_attributes_count
2632       u2 code_attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2633 
2634       unsigned int calculated_attribute_length = 0;
2635 
2636       calculated_attribute_length =
2637           sizeof(max_stack) + sizeof(max_locals) + sizeof(code_length);
2638       calculated_attribute_length +=
2639         code_length +
2640         sizeof(exception_table_length) +
2641         sizeof(code_attributes_count) +
2642         exception_table_length *
2643             ( sizeof(u2) +   // start_pc
2644               sizeof(u2) +   // end_pc
2645               sizeof(u2) +   // handler_pc
2646               sizeof(u2) );  // catch_type_index
2647 
2648       while (code_attributes_count--) {
2649         cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_NULL);  // code_attribute_name_index, code_attribute_length
2650         const u2 code_attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2651         const u4 code_attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2652         calculated_attribute_length += code_attribute_length +
2653                                        sizeof(code_attribute_name_index) +
2654                                        sizeof(code_attribute_length);
2655         check_property(valid_symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index),
2656                        "Invalid code attribute name index %u in class file %s",
2657                        code_attribute_name_index,
2658                        CHECK_NULL);
2659         if (LoadLineNumberTables &&
2660             cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_line_number_table()) {
2661           // Parse and compress line number table
2662           parse_linenumber_table(code_attribute_length,
2663                                  code_length,
2664                                  &linenumber_table,
2665                                  CHECK_NULL);
2666 
2667         } else if (LoadLocalVariableTables &&
2668                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_local_variable_table()) {
2669           // Parse local variable table
2670           if (!lvt_allocated) {
2671             localvariable_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2672               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2673             localvariable_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2674               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2675             localvariable_type_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2676               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2677             localvariable_type_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2678               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2679             lvt_allocated = true;
2680           }
2681           if (lvt_cnt == max_lvt_cnt) {
2682             max_lvt_cnt <<= 1;
2683             localvariable_table_length = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(u2, localvariable_table_length, lvt_cnt, max_lvt_cnt);
2684             localvariable_table_start  = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(const unsafe_u2*, localvariable_table_start, lvt_cnt, max_lvt_cnt);
2685           }
2686           localvariable_table_start[lvt_cnt] =
2687             parse_localvariable_table(cfs,
2688                                       code_length,
2689                                       max_locals,
2690                                       code_attribute_length,
2691                                       &localvariable_table_length[lvt_cnt],
2692                                       false,    // is not LVTT
2693                                       CHECK_NULL);
2694           total_lvt_length += localvariable_table_length[lvt_cnt];
2695           lvt_cnt++;
2696         } else if (LoadLocalVariableTypeTables &&
2697                    _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION &&
2698                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_local_variable_type_table()) {
2699           if (!lvt_allocated) {
2700             localvariable_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2701               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2702             localvariable_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2703               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2704             localvariable_type_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2705               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2706             localvariable_type_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2707               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2708             lvt_allocated = true;
2709           }
2710           // Parse local variable type table
2711           if (lvtt_cnt == max_lvtt_cnt) {
2712             max_lvtt_cnt <<= 1;
2713             localvariable_type_table_length = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(u2, localvariable_type_table_length, lvtt_cnt, max_lvtt_cnt);
2714             localvariable_type_table_start  = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(const unsafe_u2*, localvariable_type_table_start, lvtt_cnt, max_lvtt_cnt);
2715           }
2716           localvariable_type_table_start[lvtt_cnt] =
2717             parse_localvariable_table(cfs,
2718                                       code_length,
2719                                       max_locals,
2720                                       code_attribute_length,
2721                                       &localvariable_type_table_length[lvtt_cnt],
2722                                       true,     // is LVTT
2723                                       CHECK_NULL);
2724           lvtt_cnt++;
2725         } else if (_major_version >= Verifier::STACKMAP_ATTRIBUTE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
2726                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_stack_map_table()) {
2727           // Stack map is only needed by the new verifier in JDK1.5.
2728           if (parsed_stackmap_attribute) {
2729             classfile_parse_error("Multiple StackMapTable attributes in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2730           }
2731           stackmap_data = parse_stackmap_table(cfs, code_attribute_length, _need_verify, CHECK_NULL);
2732           stackmap_data_length = code_attribute_length;
2733           parsed_stackmap_attribute = true;
2734         } else {
2735           // Skip unknown attributes
2736           cfs->skip_u1(code_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2737         }
2738       }
2739       // check method attribute length
2740       if (_need_verify) {
2741         guarantee_property(method_attribute_length == calculated_attribute_length,
2742                            "Code segment has wrong length in class file %s",
2743                            CHECK_NULL);
2744       }
2745     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_exceptions()) {
2746       // Parse Exceptions attribute
2747       if (parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute) {
2748         classfile_parse_error("Multiple Exceptions attributes in class file %s",
2749                               CHECK_NULL);
2750       }
2751       parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute = true;
2752       checked_exceptions_start =
2753             parse_checked_exceptions(cfs,
2754                                      &checked_exceptions_length,
2755                                      method_attribute_length,
2756                                      CHECK_NULL);
2757     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_method_parameters()) {
2758       // reject multiple method parameters
2759       if (method_parameters_seen) {
2760         classfile_parse_error("Multiple MethodParameters attributes in class file %s",
2761                               CHECK_NULL);
2762       }
2763       method_parameters_seen = true;
2764       method_parameters_length = cfs->get_u1_fast();
2765       const u2 real_length = (method_parameters_length * 4u) + 1u;
2766       if (method_attribute_length != real_length) {
2767         classfile_parse_error(
2768           "Invalid MethodParameters method attribute length %u in class file",
2769           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2770       }
2771       method_parameters_data = cfs->current();
2772       cfs->skip_u2_fast(method_parameters_length);
2773       cfs->skip_u2_fast(method_parameters_length);
2774       // ignore this attribute if it cannot be reflected
2775       if (!SystemDictionary::Parameter_klass_loaded())
2776         method_parameters_length = -1;
2777     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
2778       if (method_attribute_length != 0) {
2779         classfile_parse_error(
2780           "Invalid Synthetic method attribute length %u in class file %s",
2781           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2782       }
2783       // Should we check that there hasn't already been a synthetic attribute?
2784       access_flags.set_is_synthetic();
2785     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) { // 4276120
2786       if (method_attribute_length != 0) {
2787         classfile_parse_error(
2788           "Invalid Deprecated method attribute length %u in class file %s",
2789           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2790       }
2791     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
2792       if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
2793         if (generic_signature_index != 0) {
2794           classfile_parse_error(
2795             "Multiple Signature attributes for method in class file %s",
2796             CHECK_NULL);
2797         }
2798         if (method_attribute_length != 2) {
2799           classfile_parse_error(
2800             "Invalid Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
2801             method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2802         }
2803         generic_signature_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_NULL);
2804       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
2805         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
2806           classfile_parse_error(
2807             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2808             CHECK_NULL);
2809         }
2810         runtime_visible_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2811         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
2812         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
2813         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2814         parse_annotations(cp,
2815                           runtime_visible_annotations,
2816                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2817                           &parsed_annotations,
2818                           _loader_data,
2819                           _can_access_vm_annotations,
2820                           CHECK_NULL);
2821         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
2822       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
2823         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
2824           classfile_parse_error(
2825             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2826             CHECK_NULL);
2827         }
2828         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
2829         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2830           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2831           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
2832           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
2833         }
2834         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2835       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_parameter_annotations()) {
2836         if (runtime_visible_parameter_annotations != NULL) {
2837           classfile_parse_error(
2838             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleParameterAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2839             CHECK_NULL);
2840         }
2841         runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2842         runtime_visible_parameter_annotations = cfs->current();
2843         assert(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations != NULL, "null visible parameter annotations");
2844         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2845       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations()) {
2846         if (runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists) {
2847           classfile_parse_error(
2848             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleParameterAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2849             CHECK_NULL);
2850         }
2851         runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists = true;
2852         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2853           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2854           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations = cfs->current();
2855           assert(runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations != NULL,
2856             "null invisible parameter annotations");
2857         }
2858         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2859       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_annotation_default()) {
2860         if (annotation_default != NULL) {
2861           classfile_parse_error(
2862             "Multiple AnnotationDefault attributes for method in class file %s",
2863             CHECK_NULL);
2864         }
2865         annotation_default_length = method_attribute_length;
2866         annotation_default = cfs->current();
2867         assert(annotation_default != NULL, "null annotation default");
2868         cfs->skip_u1(annotation_default_length, CHECK_NULL);
2869       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
2870         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
2871           classfile_parse_error(
2872             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2873             CHECK_NULL);
2874         }
2875         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2876         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
2877         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
2878         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
2879         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2880       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
2881         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
2882           classfile_parse_error(
2883             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2884             CHECK_NULL);
2885         } else {
2886           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
2887         }
2888         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2889           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2890           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
2891           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
2892         }
2893         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2894       } else {
2895         // Skip unknown attributes
2896         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2897       }
2898     } else {
2899       // Skip unknown attributes
2900       cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2901     }
2902   }
2903 
2904   if (linenumber_table != NULL) {
2905     linenumber_table->write_terminator();
2906     linenumber_table_length = linenumber_table->position();
2907   }
2908 
2909   // Make sure there's at least one Code attribute in non-native/non-abstract method
2910   if (_need_verify) {
2911     guarantee_property(access_flags.is_native() ||
2912                        access_flags.is_abstract() ||
2913                        parsed_code_attribute,
2914                        "Absent Code attribute in method that is not native or abstract in class file %s",
2915                        CHECK_NULL);
2916   }
2917 
2918   // All sizing information for a Method* is finally available, now create it
2919   InlineTableSizes sizes(
2920       total_lvt_length,
2921       linenumber_table_length,
2922       exception_table_length,
2923       checked_exceptions_length,
2924       method_parameters_length,
2925       generic_signature_index,
2926       runtime_visible_annotations_length +
2927            runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2928       runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length +
2929            runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2930       runtime_visible_type_annotations_length +
2931            runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2932       annotation_default_length,
2933       0);
2934 
2935   Method* const m = Method::allocate(_loader_data,
2936                                      code_length,
2937                                      access_flags,
2938                                      &sizes,
2939                                      ConstMethod::NORMAL,
2940                                      CHECK_NULL);
2941 
2942   ClassLoadingService::add_class_method_size(m->size()*wordSize);
2943 
2944   // Fill in information from fixed part (access_flags already set)
2945   m->set_constants(_cp);
2946   m->set_name_index(name_index);
2947   m->set_signature_index(signature_index);
2948   m->compute_from_signature(cp->symbol_at(signature_index));
2949   assert(args_size < 0 || args_size == m->size_of_parameters(), "");
2950 
2951   // Fill in code attribute information
2952   m->set_max_stack(max_stack);
2953   m->set_max_locals(max_locals);
2954   if (stackmap_data != NULL) {
2955     m->constMethod()->copy_stackmap_data(_loader_data,
2956                                          (u1*)stackmap_data,
2957                                          stackmap_data_length,
2958                                          CHECK_NULL);
2959   }
2960 
2961   // Copy byte codes
2962   m->set_code((u1*)code_start);
2963 
2964   // Copy line number table
2965   if (linenumber_table != NULL) {
2966     memcpy(m->compressed_linenumber_table(),
2967            linenumber_table->buffer(),
2968            linenumber_table_length);
2969   }
2970 
2971   // Copy exception table
2972   if (exception_table_length > 0) {
2973     Copy::conjoint_swap_if_needed<Endian::JAVA>(exception_table_start,
2974                                                 m->exception_table_start(),
2975                                                 exception_table_length * sizeof(ExceptionTableElement),
2976                                                 sizeof(u2));
2977   }
2978 
2979   // Copy method parameters
2980   if (method_parameters_length > 0) {
2981     MethodParametersElement* elem = m->constMethod()->method_parameters_start();
2982     for (int i = 0; i < method_parameters_length; i++) {
2983       elem[i].name_cp_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)method_parameters_data);
2984       method_parameters_data += 2;
2985       elem[i].flags = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)method_parameters_data);
2986       method_parameters_data += 2;
2987     }
2988   }
2989 
2990   // Copy checked exceptions
2991   if (checked_exceptions_length > 0) {
2992     Copy::conjoint_swap_if_needed<Endian::JAVA>(checked_exceptions_start,
2993                                                 m->checked_exceptions_start(),
2994                                                 checked_exceptions_length * sizeof(CheckedExceptionElement),
2995                                                 sizeof(u2));
2996   }
2997 
2998   // Copy class file LVT's/LVTT's into the HotSpot internal LVT.
2999   if (total_lvt_length > 0) {
3000     promoted_flags->set_has_localvariable_table();
3001     copy_localvariable_table(m->constMethod(),
3002                              lvt_cnt,
3003                              localvariable_table_length,
3004                              localvariable_table_start,
3005                              lvtt_cnt,
3006                              localvariable_type_table_length,
3007                              localvariable_type_table_start,
3008                              CHECK_NULL);
3009   }
3010 
3011   if (parsed_annotations.has_any_annotations())
3012     parsed_annotations.apply_to(methodHandle(THREAD, m));
3013 
3014   if (is_hidden()) { // Mark methods in hidden classes as 'hidden'.
3015     m->set_hidden(true);
3016   }
3017 
3018   // Copy annotations
3019   copy_method_annotations(m->constMethod(),
3020                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3021                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3022                           runtime_invisible_annotations,
3023                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3024                           runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
3025                           runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
3026                           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
3027                           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
3028                           runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3029                           runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3030                           runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3031                           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3032                           annotation_default,
3033                           annotation_default_length,
3034                           CHECK_NULL);
3035 
3036   if (name == vmSymbols::finalize_method_name() &&
3037       signature == vmSymbols::void_method_signature()) {
3038     if (m->is_empty_method()) {
3039       _has_empty_finalizer = true;
3040     } else {
3041       _has_finalizer = true;
3042     }
3043   }
3044   if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() &&
3045       signature == vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
3046       m->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
3047     _has_vanilla_constructor = true;
3048   }
3049 
3050   NOT_PRODUCT(m->verify());
3051   return m;
3052 }
3053 
3054 
3055 // The promoted_flags parameter is used to pass relevant access_flags
3056 // from the methods back up to the containing klass. These flag values
3057 // are added to klass's access_flags.
3058 // Side-effects: populates the _methods field in the parser
3059 void ClassFileParser::parse_methods(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3060                                     bool is_interface,
3061                                     bool is_inline_type,
3062                                     AccessFlags* promoted_flags,
3063                                     bool* has_final_method,
3064                                     bool* declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
3065                                     TRAPS) {
3066   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3067   assert(promoted_flags != NULL, "invariant");
3068   assert(has_final_method != NULL, "invariant");
3069   assert(declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods != NULL, "invariant");
3070 
3071   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
3072 
3073   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // length
3074   const u2 length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3075   if (length == 0) {
3076     _methods = Universe::the_empty_method_array();
3077   } else {
3078     _methods = MetadataFactory::new_array<Method*>(_loader_data,
3079                                                    length,
3080                                                    NULL,
3081                                                    CHECK);
3082 
3083     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3084       Method* method = parse_method(cfs,
3085                                     is_interface,
3086                                     is_inline_type,
3087                                     _cp,
3088                                     promoted_flags,
3089                                     CHECK);
3090 
3091       if (method->is_final()) {
3092         *has_final_method = true;
3093       }
3094       // declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods: declares concrete instance methods, any access flags
3095       // used for interface initialization, and default method inheritance analysis
3096       if (is_interface && !(*declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods)
3097         && !method->is_abstract() && !method->is_static()) {
3098         *declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
3099       }
3100       _methods->at_put(index, method);
3101     }
3102 
3103     if (_need_verify && length > 1) {
3104       // Check duplicated methods
3105       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3106       NameSigHash** names_and_sigs = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
3107         THREAD, NameSigHash*, HASH_ROW_SIZE);
3108       initialize_hashtable(names_and_sigs);
3109       bool dup = false;
3110       const Symbol* name = NULL;
3111       const Symbol* sig = NULL;
3112       {
3113         debug_only(NoSafepointVerifier nsv;)
3114         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
3115           const Method* const m = _methods->at(i);
3116           name = m->name();
3117           sig = m->signature();
3118           // If no duplicates, add name/signature in hashtable names_and_sigs.
3119           if (!put_after_lookup(name, sig, names_and_sigs)) {
3120             dup = true;
3121             break;
3122           }
3123         }
3124       }
3125       if (dup) {
3126         classfile_parse_error("Duplicate method name \"%s\" with signature \"%s\" in class file %s",
3127                                name->as_C_string(), sig->as_klass_external_name(), CHECK);
3128       }
3129     }
3130   }
3131 }
3132 
3133 static const intArray* sort_methods(Array<Method*>* methods) {
3134   const int length = methods->length();
3135   // If JVMTI original method ordering or sharing is enabled we have to
3136   // remember the original class file ordering.
3137   // We temporarily use the vtable_index field in the Method* to store the
3138   // class file index, so we can read in after calling qsort.
3139   // Put the method ordering in the shared archive.
3140   if (JvmtiExport::can_maintain_original_method_order() || Arguments::is_dumping_archive()) {
3141     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3142       Method* const m = methods->at(index);
3143       assert(!m->valid_vtable_index(), "vtable index should not be set");
3144       m->set_vtable_index(index);
3145     }
3146   }
3147   // Sort method array by ascending method name (for faster lookups & vtable construction)
3148   // Note that the ordering is not alphabetical, see Symbol::fast_compare
3149   Method::sort_methods(methods);
3150 
3151   intArray* method_ordering = NULL;
3152   // If JVMTI original method ordering or sharing is enabled construct int
3153   // array remembering the original ordering
3154   if (JvmtiExport::can_maintain_original_method_order() || Arguments::is_dumping_archive()) {
3155     method_ordering = new intArray(length, length, -1);
3156     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3157       Method* const m = methods->at(index);
3158       const int old_index = m->vtable_index();
3159       assert(old_index >= 0 && old_index < length, "invalid method index");
3160       method_ordering->at_put(index, old_index);
3161       m->set_vtable_index(Method::invalid_vtable_index);
3162     }
3163   }
3164   return method_ordering;
3165 }
3166 
3167 // Parse generic_signature attribute for methods and fields
3168 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_generic_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3169                                                       TRAPS) {
3170   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3171 
3172   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // generic_signature_index
3173   const u2 generic_signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3174   check_property(
3175     valid_symbol_at(generic_signature_index),
3176     "Invalid Signature attribute at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3177     generic_signature_index, CHECK_0);
3178   return generic_signature_index;
3179 }

3181 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3182                                                            TRAPS) {
3183 
3184   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3185 
3186   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // sourcefile_index
3187   const u2 sourcefile_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3188   check_property(
3189     valid_symbol_at(sourcefile_index),
3190     "Invalid SourceFile attribute at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3191     sourcefile_index, CHECK);
3192   set_class_sourcefile_index(sourcefile_index);
3193 }
3194 
3195 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3196                                                                        int length,
3197                                                                        TRAPS) {
3198   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3199 
3200   const u1* const sde_buffer = cfs->current();
3201   assert(sde_buffer != NULL, "null sde buffer");
3202 
3203   // Don't bother storing it if there is no way to retrieve it
3204   if (JvmtiExport::can_get_source_debug_extension()) {
3205     assert((length+1) > length, "Overflow checking");
3206     u1* const sde = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, u1, length+1);
3207     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
3208       sde[i] = sde_buffer[i];
3209     }
3210     sde[length] = '\0';
3211     set_class_sde_buffer((const char*)sde, length);
3212   }
3213   // Got utf8 string, set stream position forward
3214   cfs->skip_u1(length, CHECK);
3215 }
3216 
3217 
3218 // Inner classes can be static, private or protected (classic VM does this)
3219 #define RECOGNIZED_INNER_CLASS_MODIFIERS ( JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS | \
3220                                            JVM_ACC_PRIVATE |                \
3221                                            JVM_ACC_PROTECTED |              \
3222                                            JVM_ACC_STATIC                   \
3223                                          )
3224 
3225 // Return number of classes in the inner classes attribute table
3226 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3227                                                             const u1* const inner_classes_attribute_start,
3228                                                             bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute,
3229                                                             u2 enclosing_method_class_index,
3230                                                             u2 enclosing_method_method_index,
3231                                                             TRAPS) {
3232   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3233   u2 length = 0;
3234   if (inner_classes_attribute_start != NULL) {
3235     cfs->set_current(inner_classes_attribute_start);
3236     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // length
3237     length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3238   }
3239 
3240   // 4-tuples of shorts of inner classes data and 2 shorts of enclosing
3241   // method data:
3242   //   [inner_class_info_index,
3243   //    outer_class_info_index,
3244   //    inner_name_index,
3245   //    inner_class_access_flags,
3246   //    ...
3247   //    enclosing_method_class_index,
3248   //    enclosing_method_method_index]
3249   const int size = length * 4 + (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute ? 2 : 0);
3250   Array<u2>* const inner_classes = MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, size, CHECK_0);
3251   _inner_classes = inner_classes;
3252 
3253   int index = 0;
3254   cfs->guarantee_more(8 * length, CHECK_0);  // 4-tuples of u2
3255   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
3256     // Inner class index
3257     const u2 inner_class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3258     check_property(
3259       valid_klass_reference_at(inner_class_info_index),
3260       "inner_class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3261       inner_class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3262     // Outer class index
3263     const u2 outer_class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3264     check_property(
3265       outer_class_info_index == 0 ||
3266         valid_klass_reference_at(outer_class_info_index),
3267       "outer_class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3268       outer_class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3269     // Inner class name
3270     const u2 inner_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3271     check_property(
3272       inner_name_index == 0 || valid_symbol_at(inner_name_index),
3273       "inner_name_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3274       inner_name_index, CHECK_0);
3275     if (_need_verify) {
3276       guarantee_property(inner_class_info_index != outer_class_info_index,
3277                          "Class is both outer and inner class in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3278     }
3279 
3280     jint recognized_modifiers = RECOGNIZED_INNER_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
3281     // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
3282     if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
3283       recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
3284     }
3285     // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
3286     if (supports_inline_types()) {
3287       recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
3288     }
3289 
3290     // Access flags
3291     jint flags = cfs->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
3292 
3293     if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
3294       // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
3295       flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
3296     }
3297     verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK_0);
3298     AccessFlags inner_access_flags(flags);
3299 
3300     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_class_info_index);
3301     inner_classes->at_put(index++, outer_class_info_index);
3302     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_name_index);
3303     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_access_flags.as_short());
3304   }
3305 
3306   // 4347400: make sure there's no duplicate entry in the classes array
3307   if (_need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3308     for(int i = 0; i < length * 4; i += 4) {
3309       for(int j = i + 4; j < length * 4; j += 4) {
3310         guarantee_property((inner_classes->at(i)   != inner_classes->at(j) ||
3311                             inner_classes->at(i+1) != inner_classes->at(j+1) ||
3312                             inner_classes->at(i+2) != inner_classes->at(j+2) ||
3313                             inner_classes->at(i+3) != inner_classes->at(j+3)),
3314                             "Duplicate entry in InnerClasses in class file %s",
3315                             CHECK_0);
3316       }
3317     }
3318   }
3319 
3320   // Set EnclosingMethod class and method indexes.
3321   if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3322     inner_classes->at_put(index++, enclosing_method_class_index);
3323     inner_classes->at_put(index++, enclosing_method_method_index);
3324   }
3325   assert(index == size, "wrong size");
3326 
3327   // Restore buffer's current position.
3328   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3329 
3330   return length;
3331 }
3332 
3333 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3334                                                            const u1* const nest_members_attribute_start,
3335                                                            TRAPS) {
3336   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3337   u2 length = 0;
3338   if (nest_members_attribute_start != NULL) {
3339     cfs->set_current(nest_members_attribute_start);
3340     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // length
3341     length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3342   }
3343   const int size = length;
3344   Array<u2>* const nest_members = MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, size, CHECK_0);
3345   _nest_members = nest_members;
3346 
3347   int index = 0;
3348   cfs->guarantee_more(2 * length, CHECK_0);
3349   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
3350     const u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3351     check_property(
3352       valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3353       "Nest member class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3354       class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3355     nest_members->at_put(index++, class_info_index);
3356   }
3357   assert(index == size, "wrong size");
3358 
3359   // Restore buffer's current position.
3360   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3361 
3362   return length;
3363 }
3364 
3365 //  Record {
3366 //    u2 attribute_name_index;
3367 //    u4 attribute_length;
3368 //    u2 components_count;
3369 //    component_info components[components_count];
3370 //  }
3371 //  component_info {
3372 //    u2 name_index;
3373 //    u2 descriptor_index
3374 //    u2 attributes_count;
3375 //    attribute_info_attributes[attributes_count];
3376 //  }
3377 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_record_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3378                                                      const ConstantPool* cp,
3379                                                      const u1* const record_attribute_start,
3380                                                      TRAPS) {
3381   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3382   int components_count = 0;
3383   unsigned int calculate_attr_size = 0;
3384   if (record_attribute_start != NULL) {
3385     cfs->set_current(record_attribute_start);
3386     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // num of components
3387     components_count = (int)cfs->get_u2_fast();
3388     calculate_attr_size = 2;
3389   }
3390 
3391   Array<RecordComponent*>* const record_components =
3392     MetadataFactory::new_array<RecordComponent*>(_loader_data, components_count, NULL, CHECK_0);
3393   _record_components = record_components;
3394 
3395   for (int x = 0; x < components_count; x++) {
3396     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_0); // name_index, descriptor_index, attributes_count
3397 
3398     const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3399     check_property(valid_symbol_at(name_index),
3400       "Invalid constant pool index %u for name in Record attribute in class file %s",
3401       name_index, CHECK_0);
3402     const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
3403     verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK_0);
3404 
3405     const u2 descriptor_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3406     check_property(valid_symbol_at(descriptor_index),
3407       "Invalid constant pool index %u for descriptor in Record attribute in class file %s",
3408       descriptor_index, CHECK_0);
3409     const Symbol* const descr = cp->symbol_at(descriptor_index);
3410     verify_legal_field_signature(name, descr, CHECK_0);
3411 
3412     const u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3413     calculate_attr_size += 6;
3414     u2 generic_sig_index = 0;
3415     const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3416     int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3417     const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3418     int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3419     bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3420     const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3421     int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3422     const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3423     int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3424     bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3425 
3426     // Expected attributes for record components are Signature, Runtime(In)VisibleAnnotations,
3427     // and Runtime(In)VisibleTypeAnnotations.  Other attributes are ignored.
3428     for (int y = 0; y < attributes_count; y++) {
3429       cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_0);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3430       const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3431       const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3432       calculate_attr_size += 6;
3433       check_property(
3434         valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3435         "Invalid Record attribute name index %u in class file %s",
3436         attribute_name_index, CHECK_0);
3437 
3438       const Symbol* const attribute_name = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3439       if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3440         if (generic_sig_index != 0) {
3441           classfile_parse_error(
3442             "Multiple Signature attributes for Record component in class file %s",
3443             CHECK_0);
3444         }
3445         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3446           classfile_parse_error(
3447             "Invalid Signature attribute length %u in Record component in class file %s",
3448             attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3449         }
3450         generic_sig_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_0);
3451 
3452       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3453         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3454           classfile_parse_error(
3455             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3456         }
3457         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3458         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3459 
3460         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible annotation");
3461         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3462         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3463 
3464       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3465         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3466           classfile_parse_error(
3467             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3468         }
3469         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3470         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3471           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3472           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3473           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible annotation");
3474         }
3475         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3476
