3477       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3478         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3479           classfile_parse_error(
3480             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3481         }
3482         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3483         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3484 
3485         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible type annotation");
3486         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3487         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length);
3488 
3489       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3490         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3491           classfile_parse_error(
3492             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3493         }
3494         runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3495         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3496           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3497           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3498           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible type annotation");
3499         }
3500         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3501 
3502       } else {
3503         // Skip unknown attributes
3504         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3505       }
3506       calculate_attr_size += attribute_length;
3507     } // End of attributes For loop
3508 
3509     AnnotationArray* annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3510                                                         runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3511                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations,
3512                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3513                                                         CHECK_0);
3514     AnnotationArray* type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3515                                                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3516                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3517                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3518                                                              CHECK_0);
3519 
3520     RecordComponent* record_component =
3521       RecordComponent::allocate(_loader_data, name_index, descriptor_index,
3522                                 attributes_count, generic_sig_index,
3523                                 annotations, type_annotations, CHECK_0);
3524     record_components->at_put(x, record_component);
3525   }  // End of component processing loop
3526 
3527   // Restore buffer's current position.
3528   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3529   return calculate_attr_size;
3530 }
3531 
3532 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(TRAPS) {
3533   set_class_synthetic_flag(true);
3534 }
3535 
3536 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs, TRAPS) {
3537   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3538 
3539   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
3540   check_property(
3541     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
3542     "Invalid constant pool index %u in Signature attribute in class file %s",
3543     signature_index, CHECK);
3544   set_class_generic_signature_index(signature_index);
3545 }
3546 
3547 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3548                                                                   ConstantPool* cp,
3549                                                                   u4 attribute_byte_length,
3550                                                                   TRAPS) {
3551   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3552   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3553 
3554   const u1* const current_start = cfs->current();
3555 
3556   guarantee_property(attribute_byte_length >= sizeof(u2),
3557                      "Invalid BootstrapMethods attribute length %u in class file %s",
3558                      attribute_byte_length,
3559                      CHECK);
3560 
3561   cfs->guarantee_more(attribute_byte_length, CHECK);
3562 
3563   const int attribute_array_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3564 
3565   guarantee_property(_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < attribute_array_length,
3566                      "Short length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3567                      CHECK);
3568 
3569 
3570   // The attribute contains a counted array of counted tuples of shorts,
3571   // represending bootstrap specifiers:
3572   //    length*{bootstrap_method_index, argument_count*{argument_index}}
3573   const int operand_count = (attribute_byte_length - sizeof(u2)) / sizeof(u2);
3574   // operand_count = number of shorts in attr, except for leading length
3575 
3576   // The attribute is copied into a short[] array.
3577   // The array begins with a series of short[2] pairs, one for each tuple.
3578   const int index_size = (attribute_array_length * 2);
3579 
3580   Array<u2>* const operands =
3581     MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, index_size + operand_count, CHECK);
3582 
3583   // Eagerly assign operands so they will be deallocated with the constant
3584   // pool if there is an error.
3585   cp->set_operands(operands);
3586 
3587   int operand_fill_index = index_size;
3588   const int cp_size = cp->length();
3589 
3590   for (int n = 0; n < attribute_array_length; n++) {
3591     // Store a 32-bit offset into the header of the operand array.
3592     ConstantPool::operand_offset_at_put(operands, n, operand_fill_index);
3593 
3594     // Read a bootstrap specifier.
3595     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * 2, CHECK);  // bsm, argc
3596     const u2 bootstrap_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3597     const u2 argument_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3598     check_property(
3599       valid_cp_range(bootstrap_method_index, cp_size) &&
3600       cp->tag_at(bootstrap_method_index).is_method_handle(),
3601       "bootstrap_method_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3602       bootstrap_method_index,
3603       CHECK);
3604 
3605     guarantee_property((operand_fill_index + 1 + argument_count) < operands->length(),
3606       "Invalid BootstrapMethods num_bootstrap_methods or num_bootstrap_arguments value in class file %s",
3607       CHECK);
3608 
3609     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, bootstrap_method_index);
3610     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_count);
3611 
3612     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * argument_count, CHECK);  // argv[argc]
3613     for (int j = 0; j < argument_count; j++) {
3614       const u2 argument_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3615       check_property(
3616         valid_cp_range(argument_index, cp_size) &&
3617         cp->tag_at(argument_index).is_loadable_constant(),
3618         "argument_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3619         argument_index,
3620         CHECK);
3621       operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_index);
3622     }
3623   }
3624   guarantee_property(current_start + attribute_byte_length == cfs->current(),
3625                      "Bad length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3626                      CHECK);
3627 }
3628 
3629 bool ClassFileParser::supports_records() {
3630   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3631     _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3632     Arguments::enable_preview();
3633 }
3634 
3635 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_attributes(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3636                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
3637                  ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
3638                                                  TRAPS) {
3639   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3640   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3641   assert(parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
3642 
3643   // Set inner classes attribute to default sentinel
3644   _inner_classes = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3645   // Set nest members attribute to default sentinel
3646   _nest_members = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3647   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // attributes_count
3648   u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3649   bool parsed_sourcefile_attribute = false;
3650   bool parsed_innerclasses_attribute = false;
3651   bool parsed_nest_members_attribute = false;
3652   bool parsed_nest_host_attribute = false;
3653   bool parsed_record_attribute = false;
3654   bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = false;
3655   bool parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = false;
3656   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3657   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3658   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3659   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3660   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3661   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3662   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3663   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3664   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3665   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3666   bool parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = false;
3667   const u1* inner_classes_attribute_start = NULL;
3668   u4  inner_classes_attribute_length = 0;
3669   u2  enclosing_method_class_index = 0;
3670   u2  enclosing_method_method_index = 0;
3671   const u1* nest_members_attribute_start = NULL;
3672   u4  nest_members_attribute_length = 0;
3673   const u1* record_attribute_start = NULL;
3674   u4  record_attribute_length = 0;
3675 
3676   // Iterate over attributes
3677   while (attributes_count--) {
3678     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3679     const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3680     const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3681     check_property(
3682       valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3683       "Attribute name has bad constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3684       attribute_name_index, CHECK);
3685     const Symbol* const tag = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3686     if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_file()) {
3687       // Check for SourceFile tag
3688       if (_need_verify) {
3689         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong SourceFile attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3690       }
3691       if (parsed_sourcefile_attribute) {
3692         classfile_parse_error("Multiple SourceFile attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3693       } else {
3694         parsed_sourcefile_attribute = true;
3695       }
3696       parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3697     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_debug_extension()) {
3698       // Check for SourceDebugExtension tag
3699       if (parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist) {
3700           classfile_parse_error(
3701             "Multiple SourceDebugExtension attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3702       }
3703       parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = true;
3704       parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(cfs, (int)attribute_length, CHECK);
3705     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_inner_classes()) {
3706       // Check for InnerClasses tag
3707       if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute) {
3708         classfile_parse_error("Multiple InnerClasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3709       } else {
3710         parsed_innerclasses_attribute = true;
3711       }
3712       inner_classes_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3713       inner_classes_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3714       cfs->skip_u1(inner_classes_attribute_length, CHECK);
3715     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
3716       // Check for Synthetic tag
3717       // Shouldn't we check that the synthetic flags wasn't already set? - not required in spec
3718       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3719         classfile_parse_error(
3720           "Invalid Synthetic classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3721           attribute_length, CHECK);
3722       }
3723       parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(CHECK);
3724     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) {
3725       // Check for Deprecatd tag - 4276120
3726       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3727         classfile_parse_error(
3728           "Invalid Deprecated classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3729           attribute_length, CHECK);
3730       }
3731     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3732       if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3733         if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3734           classfile_parse_error(
3735             "Multiple Signature attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3736         }
3737         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3738           classfile_parse_error(
3739             "Wrong Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
3740             attribute_length, CHECK);
3741         }
3742         parse_classfile_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3743       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3744         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3745           classfile_parse_error(
3746             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3747         }
3748         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3749         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3750         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
3751         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK);
3752         parse_annotations(cp,
3753                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3754                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3755                           parsed_annotations,
3756                           _loader_data,
3757                           _can_access_vm_annotations,
3758                           CHECK);
3759         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3760       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3761         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3762           classfile_parse_error(
3763             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3764         }
3765         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3766         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3767           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3768           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3769           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
3770         }
3771         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3772       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_enclosing_method()) {
3773         if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3774           classfile_parse_error("Multiple EnclosingMethod attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3775         } else {
3776           parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = true;
3777         }
3778         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 4,
3779           "Wrong EnclosingMethod attribute length %u in class file %s",
3780           attribute_length, CHECK);
3781         cfs->guarantee_more(4, CHECK);  // class_index, method_index
3782         enclosing_method_class_index  = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3783         enclosing_method_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3784         if (enclosing_method_class_index == 0) {
3785           classfile_parse_error("Invalid class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3786         }
3787         // Validate the constant pool indices and types
3788         check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(enclosing_method_class_index),
3789           "Invalid or out-of-bounds class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3790         if (enclosing_method_method_index != 0 &&
3791             (!cp->is_within_bounds(enclosing_method_method_index) ||
3792              !cp->tag_at(enclosing_method_method_index).is_name_and_type())) {
3793           classfile_parse_error("Invalid or out-of-bounds method index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3794         }
3795       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_bootstrap_methods() &&
3796                  _major_version >= Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
3797         if (parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute) {
3798           classfile_parse_error("Multiple BootstrapMethods attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3799         }
3800         parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = true;
3801         parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(cfs, cp, attribute_length, CHECK);
3802       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3803         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3804           classfile_parse_error(
3805             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3806         }
3807         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3808         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3809         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
3810         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
3811         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK);
3812       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3813         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3814           classfile_parse_error(
3815             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3816         } else {
3817           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3818         }
3819         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3820           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3821           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3822           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
3823         }
3824         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3825       } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION) {
3826         if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_members()) {
3827           // Check for NestMembers tag
3828           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3829             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3830           } else {
3831             parsed_nest_members_attribute = true;
3832           }
3833           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3834             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestHost and NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3835           }
3836           nest_members_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3837           nest_members_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3838           cfs->skip_u1(nest_members_attribute_length, CHECK);
3839         } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_host()) {
3840           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3841             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3842           } else {
3843             parsed_nest_host_attribute = true;
3844           }
3845           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3846             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestMembers and NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3847           }
3848           if (_need_verify) {
3849             guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong NestHost attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3850           }
3851           cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);
3852           u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3853           check_property(
3854                          valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3855                          "Nest-host class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3856                          class_info_index, CHECK);
3857           _nest_host = class_info_index;
3858         } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION) {
3859           if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_record()) {
3860             // Skip over Record attribute if not supported or if super class is
3861             // not java.lang.Record.
3862             if (supports_records() &&
3863                 cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index) == vmSymbols::java_lang_Record()) {
3864               if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3865                 classfile_parse_error("Multiple Record attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3866               }
3867               // Check that class is final and not abstract.
3868               if (!_access_flags.is_final() || _access_flags.is_abstract()) {
3869                 classfile_parse_error("Record attribute in non-final or abstract class file %s", CHECK);
3870               }
3871               parsed_record_attribute = true;
3872               record_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3873               record_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3874             } else if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, record)) {
3875               // Log why the Record attribute was ignored.  Note that if the
3876               // class file version is JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION.65535 and
3877               // --enable-preview wasn't specified then a java.lang.UnsupportedClassVersionError
3878               // exception would have been thrown.
3879               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3880               if (supports_records()) {
3881                 log_info(class, record)(
3882                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because super type is not java.lang.Record",
3883                   _class_name->as_C_string());
3884               } else {
3885                 log_info(class, record)(
3886                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because class file version is not %d.65535",
3887                    _class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
3888               }
3889             }
3890             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3891           } else {
3892             // Unknown attribute
3893             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3894           }
3895         } else {
3896           // Unknown attribute
3897           cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3898         }
3899       } else {
3900         // Unknown attribute
3901         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3902       }
3903     } else {
3904       // Unknown attribute
3905       cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3906     }
3907   }
3908   _class_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3909                                             runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3910                                             runtime_invisible_annotations,
3911                                             runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3912                                             CHECK);
3913   _class_type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3914                                                  runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3915                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3916                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3917                                                  CHECK);
3918 
3919   if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute || parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3920     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(
3921                             cfs,
3922                             inner_classes_attribute_start,
3923                             parsed_innerclasses_attribute,
3924                             enclosing_method_class_index,
3925                             enclosing_method_method_index,
3926                             CHECK);
3927     if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute && _need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3928       guarantee_property(
3929         inner_classes_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + 4 * sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3930         "Wrong InnerClasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3931     }
3932   }
3933 
3934   if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3935     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(
3936                             cfs,
3937                             nest_members_attribute_start,
3938                             CHECK);
3939     if (_need_verify) {
3940       guarantee_property(
3941         nest_members_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3942         "Wrong NestMembers attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3943     }
3944   }
3945 
3946   if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3947     const unsigned int calculated_attr_length = parse_classfile_record_attribute(
3948                             cfs,
3949                             cp,
3950                             record_attribute_start,
3951                             CHECK);
3952     if (_need_verify) {
3953       guarantee_property(record_attribute_length == calculated_attr_length,
3954                          "Record attribute has wrong length in class file %s",
3955                          CHECK);
3956     }
3957   }
3958 
3959   if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index >= 0) {
3960     guarantee_property(parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute,
3961                        "Missing BootstrapMethods attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3962   }
3963 }
3964 
3965 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_attributes(InstanceKlass* k) {
3966   assert(k != NULL, "invariant");
3967 
3968   if (_synthetic_flag)
3969     k->set_is_synthetic();
3970   if (_sourcefile_index != 0) {
3971     k->set_source_file_name_index(_sourcefile_index);
3972   }
3973   if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3974     k->set_generic_signature_index(_generic_signature_index);
3975   }
3976   if (_sde_buffer != NULL) {
3977     k->set_source_debug_extension(_sde_buffer, _sde_length);
3978   }
3979 }
3980 
3981 // Create the Annotations object that will
3982 // hold the annotations array for the Klass.
3983 void ClassFileParser::create_combined_annotations(TRAPS) {
3984     if (_class_annotations == NULL &&
3985         _class_type_annotations == NULL &&
3986         _fields_annotations == NULL &&
3987         _fields_type_annotations == NULL) {
3988       // Don't create the Annotations object unnecessarily.
3989       return;
3990     }
3991 
3992     Annotations* const annotations = Annotations::allocate(_loader_data, CHECK);
3993     annotations->set_class_annotations(_class_annotations);
3994     annotations->set_class_type_annotations(_class_type_annotations);
3995     annotations->set_fields_annotations(_fields_annotations);
3996     annotations->set_fields_type_annotations(_fields_type_annotations);
3997 
3998     // This is the Annotations object that will be
3999     // assigned to InstanceKlass being constructed.
4000     _combined_annotations = annotations;
4001 
4002     // The annotations arrays below has been transfered the
4003     // _combined_annotations so these fields can now be cleared.
4004     _class_annotations       = NULL;
4005     _class_type_annotations  = NULL;
4006     _fields_annotations      = NULL;
4007     _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
4008 }
4009 
4010 // Transfer ownership of metadata allocated to the InstanceKlass.
4011 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_metadata(
4012                                             InstanceKlass* this_klass,
4013                                             int java_fields_count,
4014                                             TRAPS) {
4015   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
4016 
4017   _cp->set_pool_holder(this_klass);
4018   this_klass->set_constants(_cp);
4019   this_klass->set_fields(_fields, java_fields_count);
4020   this_klass->set_methods(_methods);
4021   this_klass->set_inner_classes(_inner_classes);
4022   this_klass->set_nest_members(_nest_members);
4023   this_klass->set_nest_host_index(_nest_host);
4024   this_klass->set_local_interfaces(_local_interfaces);
4025   this_klass->set_annotations(_combined_annotations);
4026   this_klass->set_record_components(_record_components);
4027   // Delay the setting of _transitive_interfaces until after initialize_supers() in
4028   // fill_instance_klass(). It is because the _transitive_interfaces may be shared with
4029   // its _super. If an OOM occurs while loading the current klass, its _super field
4030   // may not have been set. When GC tries to free the klass, the _transitive_interfaces
4031   // may be deallocated mistakenly in InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(). Subsequent
4032   // dereferences to the deallocated _transitive_interfaces will result in a crash.
4033 
4034   // Clear out these fields so they don't get deallocated by the destructor
4035   clear_class_metadata();
4036 }
4037 
4038 AnnotationArray* ClassFileParser::assemble_annotations(const u1* const runtime_visible_annotations,
4039                                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
4040                                                        const u1* const runtime_invisible_annotations,
4041                                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4042                                                        TRAPS) {
4043   AnnotationArray* annotations = NULL;
4044   if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL ||
4045       runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4046     annotations = MetadataFactory::new_array<u1>(_loader_data,
4047                                           runtime_visible_annotations_length +
4048                                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4049                                           CHECK_(annotations));
4050     if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
4051       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_visible_annotations_length; i++) {
4052         annotations->at_put(i, runtime_visible_annotations[i]);
4053       }
4054     }
4055     if (runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4056       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_invisible_annotations_length; i++) {
4057         int append = runtime_visible_annotations_length+i;
4058         annotations->at_put(append, runtime_invisible_annotations[i]);
4059       }
4060     }
4061   }
4062   return annotations;
4063 }
4064 
4065 const InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::parse_super_class(ConstantPool* const cp,
4066                                                         const int super_class_index,
4067                                                         const bool need_verify,
4068                                                         TRAPS) {
4069   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4070   const InstanceKlass* super_klass = NULL;
4071 
4072   if (super_class_index == 0) {
4073     check_property(_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()
4074                    || (_access_flags.get_flags() & JVM_ACC_VALUE),
4075                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4076                    super_class_index,
4077                    CHECK_NULL);
4078   } else {
4079     check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(super_class_index),
4080                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4081                    super_class_index,
4082                    CHECK_NULL);
4083     // The class name should be legal because it is checked when parsing constant pool.
4084     // However, make sure it is not an array type.
4085     bool is_array = false;
4086     if (cp->tag_at(super_class_index).is_klass()) {
4087       super_klass = InstanceKlass::cast(cp->resolved_klass_at(super_class_index));
4088       if (need_verify)
4089         is_array = super_klass->is_array_klass();
4090     } else if (need_verify) {
4091       is_array = (cp->klass_name_at(super_class_index)->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY);
4092     }
4093     if (need_verify) {
4094       guarantee_property(!is_array,
4095                         "Bad superclass name in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
4096     }
4097   }
4098   return super_klass;
4099 }
4100 
4101 #ifndef PRODUCT
4102 static void print_field_layout(const Symbol* name,
4103                                Array<u2>* fields,
4104                                ConstantPool* cp,
4105                                int instance_size,
4106                                int instance_fields_start,
4107                                int instance_fields_end,
4108                                int static_fields_end) {
4109 
4110   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
4111 
4112   tty->print("%s: field layout\n", name->as_klass_external_name());
4113   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_start, "--- instance fields start ---");
4114   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4115     if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4116       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4117         fs.offset(),
4118         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4119         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4120     }
4121   }
4122   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_end, "--- instance fields end ---");
4123   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_size * wordSize, "--- instance ends ---");
4124   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields(), "--- static fields start ---");
4125   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4126     if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4127       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4128         fs.offset(),
4129         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4130         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4131     }
4132   }
4133   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", static_fields_end, "--- static fields end ---");
4134   tty->print("\n");
4135 }
4136 #endif
4137 
4138 OopMapBlocksBuilder::OopMapBlocksBuilder(unsigned int max_blocks) {
4139   _max_nonstatic_oop_maps = max_blocks;
4140   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = 0;
4141   if (max_blocks == 0) {
4142     _nonstatic_oop_maps = NULL;
4143   } else {
4144     _nonstatic_oop_maps =
4145         NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4146     memset(_nonstatic_oop_maps, 0, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * max_blocks);
4147   }
4148 }
4149 
4150 OopMapBlock* OopMapBlocksBuilder::last_oop_map() const {
4151   assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0, "Has no oop maps");
4152   return _nonstatic_oop_maps + (_nonstatic_oop_map_count - 1);
4153 }
4154 
4155 // addition of super oop maps
4156 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::initialize_inherited_blocks(OopMapBlock* blocks, unsigned int nof_blocks) {
4157   assert(nof_blocks && _nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0 &&
4158          nof_blocks <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "invariant");
4159 
4160   memcpy(_nonstatic_oop_maps, blocks, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * nof_blocks);
4161   _nonstatic_oop_map_count += nof_blocks;
4162 }
4163 
4164 // collection of oops
4165 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::add(int offset, int count) {
4166   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0) {
4167     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4168   }
4169   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4170   if (nonstatic_oop_map->count() == 0) {  // Unused map, set it up
4171     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4172     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4173   } else if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(offset)) { // contiguous, add
4174     nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(count);
4175   } else { // Need a new one...
4176     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4177     assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "range check");
4178     nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4179     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4180     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4181   }
4182 }
4183 
4184 // general purpose copy, e.g. into allocated instanceKlass
4185 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::copy(OopMapBlock* dst) {
4186   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count != 0) {
4187     memcpy(dst, _nonstatic_oop_maps, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4188   }
4189 }
4190 
4191 // Sort and compact adjacent blocks
4192 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::compact() {
4193   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= 1) {
4194     return;
4195   }
4196   /*
4197    * Since field layout sneeks in oops before values, we will be able to condense
4198    * blocks. There is potential to compact between super, own refs and values
4199    * containing refs.
4200    *
4201    * Currently compaction is slightly limited due to values being 8 byte aligned.
4202    * This may well change: FixMe if it doesn't, the code below is fairly general purpose
4203    * and maybe it doesn't need to be.
4204    */
4205   qsort(_nonstatic_oop_maps, _nonstatic_oop_map_count, sizeof(OopMapBlock),
4206         (_sort_Fn)OopMapBlock::compare_offset);
4207   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count < 2) {
4208     return;
4209   }
4210 
4211   // Make a temp copy, and iterate through and copy back into the original
4212   ResourceMark rm;
4213   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy =
4214       NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4215   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy_end = oop_maps_copy + _nonstatic_oop_map_count;
4216   copy(oop_maps_copy);
4217   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4218   unsigned int new_count = 1;
4219   oop_maps_copy++;
4220   while(oop_maps_copy < oop_maps_copy_end) {
4221     assert(nonstatic_oop_map->offset() < oop_maps_copy->offset(), "invariant");
4222     if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(oop_maps_copy->offset())) {
4223       nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4224     } else {
4225       nonstatic_oop_map++;
4226       new_count++;
4227       nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(oop_maps_copy->offset());
4228       nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4229     }
4230     oop_maps_copy++;
4231   }
4232   assert(new_count <= _nonstatic_oop_map_count, "end up with more maps after compact() ?");
4233   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = new_count;
4234 }
4235 
4236 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_on(outputStream* st) const {
4237   st->print_cr("  OopMapBlocks: %3d  /%3d", _nonstatic_oop_map_count, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4238   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
4239     OopMapBlock* map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4240     OopMapBlock* last_map = last_oop_map();
4241     assert(map <= last_map, "Last less than first");
4242     while (map <= last_map) {
4243       st->print_cr("    Offset: %3d  -%3d Count: %3d", map->offset(),
4244                    map->offset() + map->offset_span() - heapOopSize, map->count());
4245       map++;
4246     }
4247   }
4248 }
4249 
4250 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_value_on(outputStream* st) const {
4251   print_on(st);
4252 }
4253 
4254 void ClassFileParser::throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_DECL,
4255                                                 const char* msg,
4256                                                 const Symbol* name,
4257                                                 const Symbol* sig) const {
4258 
4259   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
4260   if (name == NULL || sig == NULL) {
4261     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4262         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4263         "class: %s - %s", _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4264   }
4265   else {
4266     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4267         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4268         "\"%s\" sig: \"%s\" class: %s - %s", name->as_C_string(), sig->as_C_string(),
4269         _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4270   }
4271 }
4272 
4273 // Layout fields and fill in FieldLayoutInfo.  Could use more refactoring!
4274 void ClassFileParser::layout_fields(ConstantPool* cp,
4275                                     const FieldAllocationCount* fac,
4276                                     const ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
4277                                     FieldLayoutInfo* info,
4278                                     TRAPS) {
4279 
4280   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4281 
4282   // Field size and offset computation
4283   int nonstatic_field_size = _super_klass == NULL ? 0 :
4284                                _super_klass->nonstatic_field_size();
4285   int next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4286   int first_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4287 
4288   // Fields that are inline types are handled differently depending if they are static or not:
4289   // - static fields are oops
4290   // - non-static fields are embedded
4291 
4292   // Count the contended fields by type.
4293   //
4294   // We ignore static fields, because @Contended is not supported for them.
4295   // The layout code below will also ignore the static fields.
4296   int nonstatic_contended_count = 0;
4297   FieldAllocationCount fac_contended;
4298   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4299     FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4300     if (fs.is_contended()) {
4301       fac_contended.count[atype]++;
4302       if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4303         nonstatic_contended_count++;
4304       }
4305     }
4306   }
4307 
4308 
4309   // Calculate the starting byte offsets
4310   int next_static_oop_offset    = InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields();
4311   // Inline types in static fields are not embedded, they are handled with oops
4312   int next_static_double_offset = next_static_oop_offset +
4313                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + fac->count[STATIC_INLINE]) * heapOopSize);
4314   if (fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) {
4315     next_static_double_offset = align_up(next_static_double_offset, BytesPerLong);
4316   }
4317 
4318   int next_static_word_offset   = next_static_double_offset +
4319                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) * BytesPerLong);
4320   int next_static_short_offset  = next_static_word_offset +
4321                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_WORD]) * BytesPerInt);
4322   int next_static_byte_offset   = next_static_short_offset +
4323                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_SHORT]) * BytesPerShort);
4324 
4325   int nonstatic_fields_start  = instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() +
4326                                 nonstatic_field_size * heapOopSize;
4327 
4328   // First field of inline types is aligned on a long boundary in order to ease
4329   // in-lining of inline types (with header removal) in packed arrays and
4330   // flattened inline types
4331   int initial_inline_type_padding = 0;
4332   if (is_inline_type()) {
4333     int old = nonstatic_fields_start;
4334     nonstatic_fields_start = align_up(nonstatic_fields_start, BytesPerLong);
4335     initial_inline_type_padding = nonstatic_fields_start - old;
4336   }
4337 
4338   int next_nonstatic_field_offset = nonstatic_fields_start;
4339 
4340   const bool is_contended_class     = parsed_annotations->is_contended();
4341 
4342   // Class is contended, pad before all the fields
4343   if (is_contended_class) {
4344     next_nonstatic_field_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4345   }
4346 
4347   // Temporary inline types restrictions
4348   if (is_inline_type()) {
4349     if (is_contended_class) {
4350       throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support @Contended annotation yet");
4351       return;
4352     }
4353   }
4354 
4355   // Compute the non-contended fields count.
4356   // The packing code below relies on these counts to determine if some field
4357   // can be squeezed into the alignment gap. Contended fields are obviously
4358   // exempt from that.
4359   unsigned int nonstatic_double_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE];
4360   unsigned int nonstatic_word_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_WORD];
4361   unsigned int nonstatic_short_count  = fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT]  - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_SHORT];
4362   unsigned int nonstatic_byte_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_BYTE];
4363   unsigned int nonstatic_oop_count    = fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP]    - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_OOP];
4364 
4365   int static_inline_type_count = 0;
4366   int nonstatic_inline_type_count = 0;
4367   int* nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NULL;
4368   Klass** nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NULL;
4369   unsigned int inline_type_oop_map_count = 0;
4370   int not_flattened_inline_types = 0;
4371   int not_atomic_inline_types = 0;
4372 
4373   int max_nonstatic_inline_type = fac->count[NONSTATIC_INLINE] + 1;
4374 
4375   nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, int,
4376                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4377   for (int i = 0; i < max_nonstatic_inline_type; i++) {
4378     nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[i] = -1;
4379   }
4380   nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, Klass*,
4381                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4382 
4383   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, _cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4384     if (fs.allocation_type() == STATIC_INLINE) {
4385       ResourceMark rm;
4386       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4387         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4388       }
4389       static_inline_type_count++;
4390     } else if (fs.allocation_type() == NONSTATIC_INLINE) {
4391       // Pre-resolve the inline field and check for inline type circularity issues.
4392       ResourceMark rm;
4393       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4394         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4395       }
4396       Klass* klass =
4397         SystemDictionary::resolve_inline_field_or_fail(&fs,
4398                                                             Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
4399                                                             _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
4400       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
4401       if (!klass->access_flags().is_inline_type()) {
4402         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError());
4403       }
4404       ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4405       // Conditions to apply flattening or not should be defined in a single place
4406       bool too_big_to_flatten = (InlineFieldMaxFlatSize >= 0 &&
4407                                  (vk->size_helper() * HeapWordSize) > InlineFieldMaxFlatSize);
4408       bool too_atomic_to_flatten = vk->is_declared_atomic();
4409       bool too_volatile_to_flatten = fs.access_flags().is_volatile();
4410       if (vk->is_naturally_atomic()) {
4411         too_atomic_to_flatten = false;
4412         //too_volatile_to_flatten = false; //FIXME
4413         // volatile fields are currently never flattened, this could change in the future
4414       }
4415       if (!(too_big_to_flatten | too_atomic_to_flatten | too_volatile_to_flatten)) {
4416         nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = fs.index();
4417         nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = klass;
4418         nonstatic_inline_type_count++;
4419 
4420         ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4421         if (vklass->contains_oops()) {
4422           inline_type_oop_map_count += vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4423         }
4424         fs.set_flattened(true);
4425         if (!vk->is_atomic()) {  // flat and non-atomic: take note
4426           not_atomic_inline_types++;
4427         }
4428       } else {
4429         not_flattened_inline_types++;
4430         fs.set_flattened(false);
4431       }
4432     }
4433   }
4434 
4435   // Adjusting non_static_oop_count to take into account not flattened inline types;
4436   nonstatic_oop_count += not_flattened_inline_types;
4437 
4438   // Total non-static fields count, including every contended field
4439   unsigned int nonstatic_fields_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD] +
4440                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE] +
4441                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_INLINE];
4442 
4443   const bool super_has_nonstatic_fields =
4444           (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_nonstatic_fields());
4445   const bool has_nonstatic_fields =
4446     super_has_nonstatic_fields || (nonstatic_fields_count != 0);
4447   const bool has_nonstatic_value_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4448 
4449   if (is_inline_type() && (!has_nonstatic_fields)) {
4450     // There are a number of fixes required throughout the type system and JIT
4451     throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support zero instance size yet");
4452     return;
4453   }
4454 
4455   // Prepare list of oops for oop map generation.
4456   //
4457   // "offset" and "count" lists are describing the set of contiguous oop
4458   // regions. offset[i] is the start of the i-th region, which then has
4459   // count[i] oops following. Before we know how many regions are required,
4460   // we pessimistically allocate the maps to fit all the oops into the
4461   // distinct regions.
4462   //
4463   int super_oop_map_count = (_super_klass == NULL) ? 0 :_super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4464   int max_oop_map_count =
4465       super_oop_map_count +
4466       fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] +
4467       inline_type_oop_map_count +
4468       not_flattened_inline_types;
4469 
4470   OopMapBlocksBuilder* nonstatic_oop_maps = new OopMapBlocksBuilder(max_oop_map_count);
4471   if (super_oop_map_count > 0) {
4472     nonstatic_oop_maps->initialize_inherited_blocks(_super_klass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps(),
4473                                                     _super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count());
4474   }
4475 
4476   int first_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0; // will be set for first oop field
4477 
4478   bool compact_fields  = true;
4479   bool allocate_oops_first = false;
4480 
4481   int next_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0;
4482   int next_nonstatic_double_offset = 0;
4483 
4484   // Rearrange fields for a given allocation style
4485   if (allocate_oops_first) {
4486     // Fields order: oops, longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, padded fields
4487     next_nonstatic_oop_offset    = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4488     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset +
4489                                     (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4490   } else {
4491     // Fields order: longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, oops, padded fields
4492     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4493   }
4494 
4495   int nonstatic_oop_space_count   = 0;
4496   int nonstatic_word_space_count  = 0;
4497   int nonstatic_short_space_count = 0;
4498   int nonstatic_byte_space_count  = 0;
4499   int nonstatic_oop_space_offset = 0;
4500   int nonstatic_word_space_offset = 0;
4501   int nonstatic_short_space_offset = 0;
4502   int nonstatic_byte_space_offset = 0;
4503 
4504   // Try to squeeze some of the fields into the gaps due to
4505   // long/double alignment.
4506   if (nonstatic_double_count > 0) {
4507     int offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4508     next_nonstatic_double_offset = align_up(offset, BytesPerLong);
4509     if (compact_fields && offset != next_nonstatic_double_offset) {
4510       // Allocate available fields into the gap before double field.
4511       int length = next_nonstatic_double_offset - offset;
4512       assert(length == BytesPerInt, "");
4513       nonstatic_word_space_offset = offset;
4514       if (nonstatic_word_count > 0) {
4515         nonstatic_word_count      -= 1;
4516         nonstatic_word_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4517         length -= BytesPerInt;
4518         offset += BytesPerInt;
4519       }
4520       nonstatic_short_space_offset = offset;
4521       while (length >= BytesPerShort && nonstatic_short_count > 0) {
4522         nonstatic_short_count       -= 1;
4523         nonstatic_short_space_count += 1;
4524         length -= BytesPerShort;
4525         offset += BytesPerShort;
4526       }
4527       nonstatic_byte_space_offset = offset;
4528       while (length > 0 && nonstatic_byte_count > 0) {
4529         nonstatic_byte_count       -= 1;
4530         nonstatic_byte_space_count += 1;
4531         length -= 1;
4532       }
4533       // Allocate oop field in the gap if there are no other fields for that.
4534       nonstatic_oop_space_offset = offset;
4535       if (length >= heapOopSize && nonstatic_oop_count > 0 &&
4536           !allocate_oops_first) { // when oop fields not first
4537         nonstatic_oop_count      -= 1;
4538         nonstatic_oop_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4539         length -= heapOopSize;
4540         offset += heapOopSize;
4541       }
4542     }
4543   }
4544 
4545   int next_nonstatic_word_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset +
4546                                      (nonstatic_double_count * BytesPerLong);
4547   int next_nonstatic_short_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset +
4548                                       (nonstatic_word_count * BytesPerInt);
4549   int next_nonstatic_byte_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset +
4550                                      (nonstatic_short_count * BytesPerShort);
4551   int next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset +
4552                                        nonstatic_byte_count;
4553 
4554   // let oops jump before padding with this allocation style
4555   if (!allocate_oops_first) {
4556     next_nonstatic_oop_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4557     if( nonstatic_oop_count > 0 ) {
4558       next_nonstatic_oop_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_oop_offset, heapOopSize);
4559     }
4560     next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset + (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4561   }
4562 
4563   // Aligning embedded inline types
4564   // bug below, the current algorithm to layout embedded inline types always put them at the
4565   // end of the layout, which doesn't match the different allocation policies the VM is
4566   // supposed to provide => FixMe
4567   // Note also that the current alignment policy is to make each inline type starting on a
4568   // 64 bits boundary. This could be optimized later. For instance, it could be nice to
4569   // align inline types according to their most constrained internal type.
4570   next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4571   int next_inline_type_index = 0;
4572 
4573   // Iterate over fields again and compute correct offsets.
4574   // The field allocation type was temporarily stored in the offset slot.
4575   // oop fields are located before non-oop fields (static and non-static).
4576   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4577 
4578     // skip already laid out fields
4579     if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4580 
4581     // contended instance fields are handled below
4582     if (fs.is_contended() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4583 
4584     int real_offset = 0;
4585     const FieldAllocationType atype = (const FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4586 
4587     // pack the rest of the fields
4588     switch (atype) {
4589       // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4590       case STATIC_INLINE:   // Fallthrough
4591       case STATIC_OOP:
4592         real_offset = next_static_oop_offset;
4593         next_static_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4594         break;
4595       case STATIC_BYTE:
4596         real_offset = next_static_byte_offset;
4597         next_static_byte_offset += 1;
4598         break;
4599       case STATIC_SHORT:
4600         real_offset = next_static_short_offset;
4601         next_static_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4602         break;
4603       case STATIC_WORD:
4604         real_offset = next_static_word_offset;
4605         next_static_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4606         break;
4607       case STATIC_DOUBLE:
4608         real_offset = next_static_double_offset;
4609         next_static_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4610         break;
4611       case NONSTATIC_INLINE:
4612         if (fs.is_flattened()) {
4613           Klass* klass = nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[next_inline_type_index];
4614           assert(klass != NULL, "Klass should have been loaded and resolved earlier");
4615           assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(),"Must be an inline type");
4616           ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4617           real_offset = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4618           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset += (vklass->size_helper()) * wordSize - vklass->first_field_offset();
4619           // aligning next inline type on a 64 bits boundary
4620           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset, BytesPerLong);
4621           next_inline_type_index += 1;
4622 
4623           if (vklass->contains_oops()) { // add flatten oop maps
4624             int diff = real_offset - vklass->first_field_offset();
4625             const OopMapBlock* map = vklass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps();
4626             const OopMapBlock* const last_map = map + vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4627             while (map < last_map) {
4628               nonstatic_oop_maps->add(map->offset() + diff, map->count());
4629               map++;
4630             }
4631           }
4632           break;
4633         } else {
4634           // Fall through
4635         }
4636       case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4637         if( nonstatic_oop_space_count > 0 ) {
4638           real_offset = nonstatic_oop_space_offset;
4639           nonstatic_oop_space_offset += heapOopSize;
4640           nonstatic_oop_space_count  -= 1;
4641         } else {
4642           real_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset;
4643           next_nonstatic_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4644         }
4645         nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4646         break;
4647       case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4648         if( nonstatic_byte_space_count > 0 ) {
4649           real_offset = nonstatic_byte_space_offset;
4650           nonstatic_byte_space_offset += 1;
4651           nonstatic_byte_space_count  -= 1;
4652         } else {
4653           real_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset;
4654           next_nonstatic_byte_offset += 1;
4655         }
4656         break;
4657       case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4658         if( nonstatic_short_space_count > 0 ) {
4659           real_offset = nonstatic_short_space_offset;
4660           nonstatic_short_space_offset += BytesPerShort;
4661           nonstatic_short_space_count  -= 1;
4662         } else {
4663           real_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset;
4664           next_nonstatic_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4665         }
4666         break;
4667       case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4668         if( nonstatic_word_space_count > 0 ) {
4669           real_offset = nonstatic_word_space_offset;
4670           nonstatic_word_space_offset += BytesPerInt;
4671           nonstatic_word_space_count  -= 1;
4672         } else {
4673           real_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset;
4674           next_nonstatic_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4675         }
4676         break;
4677       case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4678         real_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4679         next_nonstatic_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4680         break;
4681       default:
4682         ShouldNotReachHere();
4683     }
4684     fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4685   }
4686 
4687 
4688   // Handle the contended cases.
4689   //
4690   // Each contended field should not intersect the cache line with another contended field.
4691   // In the absence of alignment information, we end up with pessimistically separating
4692   // the fields with full-width padding.
4693   //
4694   // Additionally, this should not break alignment for the fields, so we round the alignment up
4695   // for each field.
4696   if (nonstatic_contended_count > 0) {
4697 
4698     // if there is at least one contended field, we need to have pre-padding for them
4699     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4700 
4701     // collect all contended groups
4702     ResourceBitMap bm(cp->size());
4703     for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4704       // skip already laid out fields
4705       if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4706 
4707       if (fs.is_contended()) {
4708         bm.set_bit(fs.contended_group());
4709       }
4710     }
4711 
4712     int current_group = -1;
4713     while ((current_group = (int)bm.get_next_one_offset(current_group + 1)) != (int)bm.size()) {
4714 
4715       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4716 
4717         // skip already laid out fields
4718         if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4719 
4720         // skip non-contended fields and fields from different group
4721         if (!fs.is_contended() || (fs.contended_group() != current_group)) continue;
4722 
4723         // handle statics below
4724         if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4725 
4726         int real_offset = 0;
4727         FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4728 
4729         switch (atype) {
4730           case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4731             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, 1);
4732             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4733             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += 1;
4734             break;
4735 
4736           case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4737             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerShort);
4738             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4739             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerShort;
4740             break;
4741 
4742           case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4743             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerInt);
4744             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4745             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerInt;
4746             break;
4747 
4748           case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4749             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4750             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4751             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerLong;
4752             break;
4753 
4754             // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4755           case NONSTATIC_INLINE:
4756             throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
4757                                       "@Contended annotation not supported for inline types yet", fs.name(), fs.signature());
4758             return;
4759 
4760           case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4761             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, heapOopSize);
4762             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4763             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += heapOopSize;
4764             nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4765             break;
4766 
4767           default:
4768             ShouldNotReachHere();
4769         }
4770 
4771         if (fs.contended_group() == 0) {
4772           // Contended group defines the equivalence class over the fields:
4773           // the fields within the same contended group are not inter-padded.
4774           // The only exception is default group, which does not incur the
4775           // equivalence, and so requires intra-padding.
4776           next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4777         }
4778 
4779         fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4780       } // for
4781 
4782       // Start laying out the next group.
4783       // Note that this will effectively pad the last group in the back;
4784       // this is expected to alleviate memory contention effects for
4785       // subclass fields and/or adjacent object.
4786       // If this was the default group, the padding is already in place.
4787       if (current_group != 0) {
4788         next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4789       }
4790     }
4791 
4792     // handle static fields
4793   }
4794 
4795   // Entire class is contended, pad in the back.
4796   // This helps to alleviate memory contention effects for subclass fields
4797   // and/or adjacent object.
4798   if (is_contended_class) {
4799     assert(!is_inline_type(), "@Contended not supported for inline types yet");
4800     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4801   }
4802 
4803   int notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end;
4804   if (nonstatic_inline_type_count != 0) {
4805     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4806   } else {
4807     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4808   }
4809 
4810   int nonstatic_field_sz_align = heapOopSize;
4811   if (is_inline_type()) {
4812     if ((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) > heapOopSize) {
4813       nonstatic_field_sz_align = BytesPerLong; // value copy of fields only uses jlong copy
4814     }
4815   }
4816   int nonstatic_fields_end      = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, nonstatic_field_sz_align);
4817   int instance_end              = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, wordSize);
4818   int static_fields_end         = align_up(next_static_byte_offset, wordSize);
4819 
4820   int static_field_size         = (static_fields_end -
4821                                    InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields()) / wordSize;
4822   nonstatic_field_size          = nonstatic_field_size +
4823                                   (nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) / heapOopSize;
4824 
4825   int instance_size             = align_object_size(instance_end / wordSize);
4826 
4827   assert(instance_size == align_object_size(align_up(
4828          (instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() + nonstatic_field_size*heapOopSize)
4829          + initial_inline_type_padding, wordSize) / wordSize), "consistent layout helper value");
4830 
4831 
4832   // Invariant: nonstatic_field end/start should only change if there are
4833   // nonstatic fields in the class, or if the class is contended. We compare
4834   // against the non-aligned value, so that end alignment will not fail the
4835   // assert without actually having the fields.
4836   assert((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end == nonstatic_fields_start) ||
4837          is_contended_class ||
4838          (nonstatic_fields_count > 0), "double-check nonstatic start/end");
4839 
4840   // Number of non-static oop map blocks allocated at end of klass.
4841   nonstatic_oop_maps->compact();
4842 
4843 #ifndef PRODUCT
4844   if ((PrintFieldLayout && !is_inline_type()) ||
4845       (PrintInlineLayout && (is_inline_type() || has_nonstatic_value_fields))) {
4846     print_field_layout(_class_name,
4847           _fields,
4848           cp,
4849           instance_size,
4850           nonstatic_fields_start,
4851           nonstatic_fields_end,
4852           static_fields_end);
4853     nonstatic_oop_maps->print_on(tty);
4854     tty->print("\n");
4855     tty->print_cr("Instance size = %d", instance_size);
4856     tty->print_cr("Nonstatic_field_size = %d", nonstatic_field_size);
4857     tty->print_cr("Static_field_size = %d", static_field_size);
4858     tty->print_cr("Has nonstatic fields = %d", has_nonstatic_fields);
4859     tty->print_cr("---");
4860   }
4861 
4862 #endif
4863   // Pass back information needed for InstanceKlass creation
4864   info->oop_map_blocks = nonstatic_oop_maps;
4865   info->_instance_size = instance_size;
4866   info->_static_field_size = static_field_size;
4867   info->_nonstatic_field_size = nonstatic_field_size;
4868   info->_has_nonstatic_fields = has_nonstatic_fields;
4869   info->_has_inline_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4870 
4871   // An inline type is naturally atomic if it has just one field, and
4872   // that field is simple enough.
4873   info->_is_naturally_atomic = (is_inline_type() &&
4874                                 !super_has_nonstatic_fields &&
4875                                 (nonstatic_fields_count <= 1) &&
4876                                 (not_atomic_inline_types == 0) &&
4877                                 (nonstatic_contended_count == 0));
4878   // This may be too restrictive, since if all the fields fit in 64
4879   // bits we could make the decision to align instances of this class
4880   // to 64-bit boundaries, and load and store them as single words.
4881   // And on machines which supported larger atomics we could similarly
4882   // allow larger values to be atomic, if properly aligned.
4883 }
4884 
4885 void ClassFileParser::set_precomputed_flags(InstanceKlass* ik) {
4886   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
4887 
4888   const Klass* const super = ik->super();
4889 
4890   // Check if this klass has an empty finalize method (i.e. one with return bytecode only),
4891   // in which case we don't have to register objects as finalizable
4892   if (!_has_empty_finalizer) {
4893     if (_has_finalizer ||
4894         (super != NULL && super->has_finalizer())) {
4895       ik->set_has_finalizer();
4896     }
4897   }
4898 
4899 #ifdef ASSERT
4900   bool f = false;
4901   const Method* const m = ik->lookup_method(vmSymbols::finalize_method_name(),
4902                                            vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4903   if (m != NULL && !m->is_empty_method()) {
4904       f = true;
4905   }
4906 
4907   // Spec doesn't prevent agent from redefinition of empty finalizer.
4908   // Despite the fact that it's generally bad idea and redefined finalizer
4909   // will not work as expected we shouldn't abort vm in this case
4910   if (!ik->has_redefined_this_or_super()) {
4911     assert(ik->has_finalizer() == f, "inconsistent has_finalizer");
4912   }
4913 #endif
4914 
4915   // Check if this klass supports the java.lang.Cloneable interface
4916   if (SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass_loaded()) {
4917     if (ik->is_subtype_of(SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass())) {
4918       if (ik->is_value()) {
4919         Thread *THREAD = Thread::current();
4920         throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support Cloneable");
4921         return;
4922       }
4923       ik->set_is_cloneable();
4924     }
4925   }
4926 
4927   // Check if this klass has a vanilla default constructor
4928   if (super == NULL) {
4929     // java.lang.Object has empty default constructor
4930     ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4931   } else {
4932     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor() &&
4933         _has_vanilla_constructor) {
4934       ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4935     }
4936 #ifdef ASSERT
4937     bool v = false;
4938     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor()) {
4939       const Method* const constructor =
4940         ik->find_method(vmSymbols::object_initializer_name(),
4941                        vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4942       if (constructor != NULL && constructor->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
4943         v = true;
4944       }
4945     }
4946     assert(v == ik->has_vanilla_constructor(), "inconsistent has_vanilla_constructor");
4947 #endif
4948   }
4949 
4950   // If it cannot be fast-path allocated, set a bit in the layout helper.
4951   // See documentation of InstanceKlass::can_be_fastpath_allocated().
4952   assert(ik->size_helper() > 0, "layout_helper is initialized");
4953   if ((!RegisterFinalizersAtInit && ik->has_finalizer())
4954       || ik->is_abstract() || ik->is_interface()
4955       || (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Class() && ik->class_loader() == NULL)
4956       || ik->size_helper() >= FastAllocateSizeLimit) {
4957     // Forbid fast-path allocation.
4958     const jint lh = Klass::instance_layout_helper(ik->size_helper(), true);
4959     ik->set_layout_helper(lh);
4960   }
4961 }
4962 
4963 bool ClassFileParser::supports_inline_types() const {
4964   // Inline types are only supported by class file version 55 and later
4965   return _major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION;
4966 }
4967 
4968 // utility methods for appending an array with check for duplicates
4969 
4970 static void append_interfaces(GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* result,
4971                               const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const ifs) {
4972   // iterate over new interfaces
4973   for (int i = 0; i < ifs->length(); i++) {
4974     InstanceKlass* const e = ifs->at(i);
4975     assert(e->is_klass() && e->is_interface(), "just checking");
4976     // add new interface
4977     result->append_if_missing(e);
4978   }
4979 }
4980 
4981 static Array<InstanceKlass*>* compute_transitive_interfaces(const InstanceKlass* super,
4982                                                             Array<InstanceKlass*>* local_ifs,
4983                                                             ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
4984                                                             TRAPS) {
4985   assert(local_ifs != NULL, "invariant");
4986   assert(loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
4987 
4988   // Compute maximum size for transitive interfaces
4989   int max_transitive_size = 0;
4990   int super_size = 0;
4991   // Add superclass transitive interfaces size
4992   if (super != NULL) {
4993     super_size = super->transitive_interfaces()->length();
4994     max_transitive_size += super_size;
4995   }
4996   // Add local interfaces' super interfaces
4997   const int local_size = local_ifs->length();
4998   for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
4999     InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5000     max_transitive_size += l->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5001   }
5002   // Finally add local interfaces
5003   max_transitive_size += local_size;
5004   // Construct array
5005   if (max_transitive_size == 0) {
5006     // no interfaces, use canonicalized array
5007     return Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
5008   } else if (max_transitive_size == super_size) {
5009     // no new local interfaces added, share superklass' transitive interface array
5010     return super->transitive_interfaces();
5011     // The three lines below are commented to work around bug JDK-8245487
5012 //  } else if (max_transitive_size == local_size) {
5013 //    // only local interfaces added, share local interface array
5014 //    return local_ifs;
5015   } else {
5016     ResourceMark rm;
5017     GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* const result = new GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>(max_transitive_size);
5018 
5019     // Copy down from superclass
5020     if (super != NULL) {
5021       append_interfaces(result, super->transitive_interfaces());
5022     }
5023 
5024     // Copy down from local interfaces' superinterfaces
5025     for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5026       InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5027       append_interfaces(result, l->transitive_interfaces());
5028     }
5029     // Finally add local interfaces
5030     append_interfaces(result, local_ifs);
5031 
5032     // length will be less than the max_transitive_size if duplicates were removed
5033     const int length = result->length();
5034     assert(length <= max_transitive_size, "just checking");
5035 
5036     if (length == 1 && result->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
5037       return Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
5038     }
5039 
5040     Array<InstanceKlass*>* const new_result =
5041       MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(loader_data, length, CHECK_NULL);
5042     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
5043       InstanceKlass* const e = result->at(i);
5044       assert(e != NULL, "just checking");
5045       new_result->at_put(i, e);
5046     }
5047     return new_result;
5048   }
5049 }
5050 
5051 static void check_super_class_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5052   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5053   const Klass* const super = this_klass->super();
5054 
5055   if (super != NULL) {
5056 
5057     // If the loader is not the boot loader then throw an exception if its
5058     // superclass is in package jdk.internal.reflect and its loader is not a
5059     // special reflection class loader
5060     if (!this_klass->class_loader_data()->is_the_null_class_loader_data()) {
5061       assert(super->is_instance_klass(), "super is not instance klass");
5062       PackageEntry* super_package = super->package();
5063       if (super_package != NULL &&
5064           super_package->name()->fast_compare(vmSymbols::jdk_internal_reflect()) == 0 &&
5065           !java_lang_ClassLoader::is_reflection_class_loader(this_klass->class_loader())) {
5066         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5067         Exceptions::fthrow(
5068           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5069           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5070           "class %s loaded by %s cannot access jdk/internal/reflect superclass %s",
5071           this_klass->external_name(),
5072           this_klass->class_loader_data()->loader_name_and_id(),
5073           super->external_name());
5074         return;
5075       }
5076     }
5077 
5078     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5079       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, InstanceKlass::cast(super), false);
5080     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5081       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5082       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5083                                                       InstanceKlass::cast(super),
5084                                                       vca_result);
5085       if (msg == NULL) {
5086         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == super->module());
5087         Exceptions::fthrow(
5088           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5089           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5090           "class %s cannot access its %ssuperclass %s (%s%s%s)",
5091           this_klass->external_name(),
5092           super->is_abstract() ? "abstract " : "",
5093           super->external_name(),
5094           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(super) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5095           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5096           (same_module) ? "" : super->class_in_module_of_loader());
5097       } else {
5098         // Add additional message content.
5099         Exceptions::fthrow(
5100           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5101           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5102           "superclass access check failed: %s",
5103           msg);
5104       }
5105     }
5106   }
5107 }
5108 
5109 
5110 static void check_super_interface_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5111   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5112   const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = this_klass->local_interfaces();
5113   const int lng = local_interfaces->length();
5114   for (int i = lng - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
5115     InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
5116     assert (k != NULL && k->is_interface(), "invalid interface");
5117     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5118       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, k, false);
5119     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5120       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5121       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5122                                                       k,
