6477 ClassFileParser::ClassFileParser(ClassFileStream* stream,
6478                                  Symbol* name,
6479                                  ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
6480                                  const ClassLoadInfo* cl_info,
6481                                  Publicity pub_level,
6482                                  TRAPS) :
6483   _stream(stream),
6484   _class_name(NULL),
6485   _loader_data(loader_data),
6486   _unsafe_anonymous_host(cl_info->unsafe_anonymous_host()),
6487   _cp_patches(cl_info->cp_patches()),
6488   _is_hidden(cl_info->is_hidden()),
6489   _can_access_vm_annotations(cl_info->can_access_vm_annotations()),
6490   _num_patched_klasses(0),
6491   _max_num_patched_klasses(0),
6492   _orig_cp_size(0),
6493   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index(0),
6494   _super_klass(),
6495   _cp(NULL),
6496   _fields(NULL),
6497   _methods(NULL),
6498   _inner_classes(NULL),
6499   _nest_members(NULL),
6500   _nest_host(0),
6501   _record_components(NULL),
6502   _temp_local_interfaces(NULL),
6503   _local_interfaces(NULL),
6504   _transitive_interfaces(NULL),
6505   _combined_annotations(NULL),
6506   _class_annotations(NULL),
6507   _class_type_annotations(NULL),
6508   _fields_annotations(NULL),
6509   _fields_type_annotations(NULL),
6510   _klass(NULL),
6511   _klass_to_deallocate(NULL),
6512   _parsed_annotations(NULL),
6513   _fac(NULL),
6514   _field_info(NULL),
6515   _method_ordering(NULL),
6516   _all_mirandas(NULL),
6517   _vtable_size(0),
6518   _itable_size(0),
6519   _num_miranda_methods(0),
6520   _rt(REF_NONE),
6521   _protection_domain(cl_info->protection_domain()),
6522   _access_flags(),
6523   _pub_level(pub_level),
6524   _bad_constant_seen(0),
6525   _synthetic_flag(false),
6526   _sde_length(false),
6527   _sde_buffer(NULL),
6528   _sourcefile_index(0),
6529   _generic_signature_index(0),
6530   _major_version(0),
6531   _minor_version(0),
6532   _this_class_index(0),
6533   _super_class_index(0),
6534   _itfs_len(0),
6535   _java_fields_count(0),
6536   _need_verify(false),
6537   _relax_verify(false),
6538   _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6539   _declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6540   _has_final_method(false),
6541   _has_contended_fields(false),
6542   _has_inline_fields(false),
6543   _has_nonstatic_fields(false),
6544   _is_empty_inline_type(false),
6545   _is_naturally_atomic(false),
6546   _is_declared_atomic(false),
6547   _invalid_inline_super(false),
6548   _invalid_identity_super(false),
6549   _implements_identityObject(false),
6550   _has_injected_identityObject(false),
6551   _has_finalizer(false),
6552   _has_empty_finalizer(false),
6553   _has_vanilla_constructor(false),
6554   _max_bootstrap_specifier_index(-1) {
6555 
6556   _class_name = name != NULL ? name : vmSymbols::unknown_class_name();
6557   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6558 
6559   assert(THREAD->is_Java_thread(), "invariant");
6560   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6561   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6562   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
6563   assert(_stream->buffer() == _stream->current(), "invariant");
6564   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6565   assert(0 == _access_flags.as_int(), "invariant");
6566 
6567   // Figure out whether we can skip format checking (matching classic VM behavior)
6568   if (DumpSharedSpaces) {
6569     // verify == true means it's a 'remote' class (i.e., non-boot class)
6570     // Verification decision is based on BytecodeVerificationRemote flag
6571     // for those classes.
6572     _need_verify = (stream->need_verify()) ? BytecodeVerificationRemote :
6573                                               BytecodeVerificationLocal;
6574   }
6575   else {
6576     _need_verify = Verifier::should_verify_for(_loader_data->class_loader(),
6577                                                stream->need_verify());
6578   }
6579   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
6580     int len = _cp_patches->length();
6581     for (int i=0; i<len; i++) {
6582       if (has_cp_patch_at(i)) {
6583         Handle patch = cp_patch_at(i);
6584         if (java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()) || java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
6585           // We need to append the names of the patched classes to the end of the constant pool,
6586           // because a patched class may have a Utf8 name that's not already included in the
6587           // original constant pool. These class names are used when patch_constant_pool()
6588           // calls patch_class().
6589           //
6590           // Note that a String in cp_patch_at(i) may be used to patch a Utf8, a String, or a Class.
6591           // At this point, we don't know the tag for index i yet, because we haven't parsed the
6592           // constant pool. So we can only assume the worst -- every String is used to patch a Class.
6593           _max_num_patched_klasses++;
6594         }
6595       }
6596     }
6597   }
6598 
6599   // synch back verification state to stream
6600   stream->set_verify(_need_verify);
6601 
6602   // Check if verification needs to be relaxed for this class file
6603   // Do not restrict it to jdk1.0 or jdk1.1 to maintain backward compatibility (4982376)
6604   _relax_verify = relax_format_check_for(_loader_data);
6605 
6606   parse_stream(stream, CHECK);
6607 
6608   post_process_parsed_stream(stream, _cp, CHECK);
6609 }
6610 
6611 void ClassFileParser::clear_class_metadata() {
6612   // metadata created before the instance klass is created.  Must be
6613   // deallocated if classfile parsing returns an error.
6614   _cp = NULL;
6615   _fields = NULL;
6616   _methods = NULL;
6617   _inner_classes = NULL;
6618   _nest_members = NULL;
6619   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6620   _combined_annotations = NULL;
6621   _class_annotations = _class_type_annotations = NULL;
6622   _fields_annotations = _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
6623   _record_components = NULL;
6624 }
6625 
6626 // Destructor to clean up
6627 ClassFileParser::~ClassFileParser() {
6628   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6629 
6630   if (_cp != NULL) {
6631     MetadataFactory::free_metadata(_loader_data, _cp);
6632   }
6633   if (_fields != NULL) {
6634     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _fields);
6635   }
6636 
6637   if (_methods != NULL) {
6638     // Free methods
6639     InstanceKlass::deallocate_methods(_loader_data, _methods);
6640   }
6641 
6642   // beware of the Universe::empty_blah_array!!
6643   if (_inner_classes != NULL && _inner_classes != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6644     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _inner_classes);
6645   }
6646 
6647   if (_nest_members != NULL && _nest_members != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6648     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _nest_members);
6649   }
6650 
6651   if (_record_components != NULL) {
6652     InstanceKlass::deallocate_record_components(_loader_data, _record_components);
6653   }
6654 
6655   // Free interfaces
6656   InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(_loader_data, _super_klass,
6657                                        _local_interfaces, _transitive_interfaces);
6658 
6659   if (_combined_annotations != NULL) {
6660     // After all annotations arrays have been created, they are installed into the
6661     // Annotations object that will be assigned to the InstanceKlass being created.
6662 
6663     // Deallocate the Annotations object and the installed annotations arrays.
6664     _combined_annotations->deallocate_contents(_loader_data);
6665 
6666     // If the _combined_annotations pointer is non-NULL,
6667     // then the other annotations fields should have been cleared.
6668     assert(_class_annotations       == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6669     assert(_class_type_annotations  == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6670     assert(_fields_annotations      == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6671     assert(_fields_type_annotations == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6672   } else {
6673     // If the annotations arrays were not installed into the Annotations object,
6674     // then they have to be deallocated explicitly.
6675     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_annotations);
6676     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_type_annotations);
6677     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_annotations);
6678     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_type_annotations);
6679   }
6680 
6681   clear_class_metadata();
6682   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6683 
6684   // deallocate the klass if already created.  Don't directly deallocate, but add
6685   // to the deallocate list so that the klass is removed from the CLD::_klasses list
6686   // at a safepoint.
6687   if (_klass_to_deallocate != NULL) {
6688     _loader_data->add_to_deallocate_list(_klass_to_deallocate);
6689   }
6690 }
6691 
6692 void ClassFileParser::parse_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6693                                    TRAPS) {
6694 
6695   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6696   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6697 
6698   // BEGIN STREAM PARSING
6699   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // magic, major, minor
6700   // Magic value
6701   const u4 magic = stream->get_u4_fast();
6702   guarantee_property(magic == JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC,
6703                      "Incompatible magic value %u in class file %s",
6704                      magic, CHECK);
6705 
6706   // Version numbers
6707   _minor_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6708   _major_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6709 
6710   if (DumpSharedSpaces && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6711     ResourceMark rm;
6712     warning("Pre JDK 6 class not supported by CDS: %u.%u %s",
6713             _major_version,  _minor_version, _class_name->as_C_string());
6714     Exceptions::fthrow(
6715       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6716       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
6717       "Unsupported major.minor version for dump time %u.%u",
6718       _major_version,
6719       _minor_version);
6720   }
6721 
6722   // Check version numbers - we check this even with verifier off
6723   verify_class_version(_major_version, _minor_version, _class_name, CHECK);
6724 
6725   stream->guarantee_more(3, CHECK); // length, first cp tag
6726   u2 cp_size = stream->get_u2_fast();
6727 
6728   guarantee_property(
6729     cp_size >= 1, "Illegal constant pool size %u in class file %s",
6730     cp_size, CHECK);
6731 
6732   _orig_cp_size = cp_size;
6733   if (is_hidden()) { // Add a slot for hidden class name.
6734     assert(_max_num_patched_klasses == 0, "Sanity check");
6735     cp_size++;
6736   } else {
6737     if (int(cp_size) + _max_num_patched_klasses > 0xffff) {
6738       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_InternalError(), "not enough space for patched classes");
6739     }
6740     cp_size += _max_num_patched_klasses;
6741   }
6742 
6743   _cp = ConstantPool::allocate(_loader_data,
6744                                cp_size,
6745                                CHECK);
6746 
6747   ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
6748 
6749   parse_constant_pool(stream, cp, _orig_cp_size, CHECK);
6750 
6751   assert(cp_size == (const u2)cp->length(), "invariant");
6752 
6753   // ACCESS FLAGS
6754   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
6755 
6756   jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
6757   // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
6758   if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
6759     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
6760   }
6761   // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
6762   if (supports_inline_types()) {
6763     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
6764   }
6765 
6766   // Access flags
6767   jint flags = stream->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
6768 
6769   if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6770     // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
6771     flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
6772   }
6773 
6774   verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK);
6775 
6776   short bad_constant = class_bad_constant_seen();
6777   if (bad_constant != 0) {
6778     // Do not throw CFE until after the access_flags are checked because if
6779     // ACC_MODULE is set in the access flags, then NCDFE must be thrown, not CFE.
6780     classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s", bad_constant, CHECK);
6781   }
6782 
6783   _access_flags.set_flags(flags);
6784 
6785   // This class and superclass
6786   _this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6787   check_property(
6788     valid_cp_range(_this_class_index, cp_size) &&
6789       cp->tag_at(_this_class_index).is_unresolved_klass(),
6790     "Invalid this class index %u in constant pool in class file %s",
6791     _this_class_index, CHECK);
6792 
6793   Symbol* const class_name_in_cp = cp->klass_name_at(_this_class_index);
6794   assert(class_name_in_cp != NULL, "class_name can't be null");
6795 
6796   // Don't need to check whether this class name is legal or not.
6797   // It has been checked when constant pool is parsed.
6798   // However, make sure it is not an array type.
6799   if (_need_verify) {
6800     guarantee_property(class_name_in_cp->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
6801                        "Bad class name in class file %s",
6802                        CHECK);
6803   }
6804 
6805 #ifdef ASSERT
6806   // Basic sanity checks
6807   assert(!(_is_hidden && (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL)), "mutually exclusive variants");
6808 
6809   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6810     assert(_class_name == vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "A named anonymous class???");
6811   }
6812   if (_is_hidden) {
6813     assert(_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "hidden classes should have a special name");
6814   }
6815 #endif
6816 
6817   // Update the _class_name as needed depending on whether this is a named,
6818   // un-named, hidden or unsafe-anonymous class.
6819 
6820   if (_is_hidden) {
6821     assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
6822 #ifdef ASSERT
6823     if (_need_verify) {
6824       verify_legal_class_name(_class_name, CHECK);
6825     }
6826 #endif
6827 
6828   // NOTE: !_is_hidden does not imply "findable" as it could be an old-style
6829   //       "hidden" unsafe-anonymous class
6830 
6831   // If this is an anonymous class fix up its name if it is in the unnamed
6832   // package.  Otherwise, throw IAE if it is in a different package than
6833   // its host class.
6834   } else if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6835     update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6836     fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(CHECK);
6837 
6838   } else {
6839     // Check if name in class file matches given name
6840     if (_class_name != class_name_in_cp) {
6841       if (_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name()) {
6842         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6843         Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6844                            vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
6845                            "%s (wrong name: %s)",
6846                            class_name_in_cp->as_C_string(),
6847                            _class_name->as_C_string()
6848                            );
6849         return;
6850       } else {
6851         // The class name was not known by the caller so we set it from
6852         // the value in the CP.
6853         update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6854       }
6855       // else nothing to do: the expected class name matches what is in the CP
6856     }
6857   }
6858 
6859   // Verification prevents us from creating names with dots in them, this
6860   // asserts that that's the case.
6861   assert(is_internal_format(_class_name), "external class name format used internally");
6862 
6863   if (!is_internal()) {
6864     LogTarget(Debug, class, preorder) lt;
6865     if (lt.is_enabled()){
6866       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6867       LogStream ls(lt);
6868       ls.print("%s", _class_name->as_klass_external_name());
6869       if (stream->source() != NULL) {
6870         ls.print(" source: %s", stream->source());
6871       }
6872       ls.cr();
6873     }
6874 
6875 #if INCLUDE_CDS
6876     if (DumpLoadedClassList != NULL && stream->source() != NULL && classlist_file->is_open()) {
6877       if (!ClassLoader::has_jrt_entry()) {
6878         warning("DumpLoadedClassList and CDS are not supported in exploded build");
6879         DumpLoadedClassList = NULL;
6880       } else if (SystemDictionaryShared::is_sharing_possible(_loader_data) &&
6881                  !_is_hidden &&
6882                  _unsafe_anonymous_host == NULL) {
6883         // Only dump the classes that can be stored into CDS archive.
6884         // Hidden and unsafe anonymous classes such as generated LambdaForm classes are also not included.
6885         oop class_loader = _loader_data->class_loader();
6886         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6887         bool skip = false;
6888         if (class_loader == NULL || SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(class_loader)) {
6889           // For the boot and platform class loaders, skip classes that are not found in the
6890           // java runtime image, such as those found in the --patch-module entries.
6891           // These classes can't be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6892           if (!stream->from_boot_loader_modules_image() && strncmp(stream->source(), "jrt:", 4) != 0) {
6893             skip = true;
6894           }
6895 
6896           if (class_loader == NULL && ClassLoader::contains_append_entry(stream->source())) {
6897             // .. but don't skip the boot classes that are loaded from -Xbootclasspath/a
6898             // as they can be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6899             skip = false;
6900           }
6901         }
6902         if (skip) {
6903           tty->print_cr("skip writing class %s from source %s to classlist file",
6904             _class_name->as_C_string(), stream->source());
6905         } else {
6906           classlist_file->print_cr("%s", _class_name->as_C_string());
6907           classlist_file->flush();
6908         }
6909       }
6910     }
6911 #endif
6912   }
6913 
6914   // SUPERKLASS
6915   _super_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6916   _super_klass = parse_super_class(cp,
6917                                    _super_class_index,
6918                                    _need_verify,
6919                                    CHECK);
6920 
6921   // Interfaces
6922   _itfs_len = stream->get_u2_fast();
6923   parse_interfaces(stream,
6924                    _itfs_len,
6925                    cp,
6926                    is_inline_type(),
6927                    &_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6928                    &_is_declared_atomic,
6929                    CHECK);
6930 
6931   assert(_temp_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
6932 
6933   // Fields (offsets are filled in later)
6934   _fac = new FieldAllocationCount();
6935   parse_fields(stream,
6936                is_interface(),
6937                is_inline_type(),
6938                _fac,
6939                cp,
6940                cp_size,
6941                &_java_fields_count,
6942                CHECK);
6943 
6944   assert(_fields != NULL, "invariant");
6945 
6946   // Methods
6947   AccessFlags promoted_flags;
6948   parse_methods(stream,
6949                 is_interface(),
6950                 is_inline_type(),
6951                 &promoted_flags,
6952                 &_has_final_method,
6953                 &_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6954                 CHECK);
6955 
6956   assert(_methods != NULL, "invariant");
6957 
6958   // promote flags from parse_methods() to the klass' flags
6959   _access_flags.add_promoted_flags(promoted_flags.as_int());
6960 
6961   if (_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6962     _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
6963   }
6964 
6965   // Additional attributes/annotations
6966   _parsed_annotations = new ClassAnnotationCollector();
6967   parse_classfile_attributes(stream, cp, _parsed_annotations, CHECK);
6968 
6969   assert(_inner_classes != NULL, "invariant");
6970 
6971   // Finalize the Annotations metadata object,
6972   // now that all annotation arrays have been created.
6973   create_combined_annotations(CHECK);
6974 
6975   // Make sure this is the end of class file stream
6976   guarantee_property(stream->at_eos(),
6977                      "Extra bytes at the end of class file %s",
6978                      CHECK);
6979 
6980   // all bytes in stream read and parsed
6981 }
6982 
6983 void ClassFileParser::mangle_hidden_class_name(InstanceKlass* const ik) {
6984   ResourceMark rm;
6985   // Construct hidden name from _class_name, "+", and &ik. Note that we can't
6986   // use a '/' because that confuses finding the class's package.  Also, can't
6987   // use an illegal char such as ';' because that causes serialization issues
6988   // and issues with hidden classes that create their own hidden classes.
6989   char addr_buf[20];
6990   jio_snprintf(addr_buf, 20, INTPTR_FORMAT, p2i(ik));
6991   size_t new_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length() + 2 + strlen(addr_buf);
6992   char* new_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, new_name_len);
6993   jio_snprintf(new_name, new_name_len, "%s+%s",
6994                _class_name->as_C_string(), addr_buf);
6995   update_class_name(SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_name));
6996 
6997   // Add a Utf8 entry containing the hidden name.
6998   assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
6999   int hidden_index = _orig_cp_size; // this is an extra slot we added
7000   _cp->symbol_at_put(hidden_index, _class_name);
7001 
7002   // Update this_class_index's slot in the constant pool with the new Utf8 entry.
7003   // We have to update the resolved_klass_index and the name_index together
7004   // so extract the existing resolved_klass_index first.
7005   CPKlassSlot cp_klass_slot = _cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index);
7006   int resolved_klass_index = cp_klass_slot.resolved_klass_index();
7007   _cp->unresolved_klass_at_put(_this_class_index, hidden_index, resolved_klass_index);
7008   assert(_cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index).name_index() == _orig_cp_size,
7009          "Bad name_index");
7010 }
7011 
7012 void ClassFileParser::post_process_parsed_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
7013                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
7014                                                  TRAPS) {
7015   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
7016   assert(stream->at_eos(), "invariant");
7017   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
7018   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
7019 
7020   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
7021     check_property(_temp_local_interfaces->length() == 0,
7022         "java.lang.Object cannot implement an interface in class file %s",
7023         CHECK);
7024   }
7025   // We check super class after class file is parsed and format is checked
7026   if (_super_class_index > 0 && NULL ==_super_klass) {
7027     Symbol* const super_class_name = cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index);
7028     if (is_interface()) {
7029       // Before attempting to resolve the superclass, check for class format
7030       // errors not checked yet.
7031       guarantee_property(super_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object(),
7032         "Interfaces must have java.lang.Object as superclass in class file %s",
7033         CHECK);
7034     }
7035     Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7036     _super_klass = (const InstanceKlass*)
7037                        SystemDictionary::resolve_super_or_fail(_class_name,
7038                                                                super_class_name,
7039                                                                loader,
7040                                                                _protection_domain,
7041                                                                true,
7042                                                                CHECK);
7043   }
7044 
7045   if (_super_klass != NULL) {
7046     if (_super_klass->has_nonstatic_concrete_methods()) {
7047       _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
7048     }
7049     if (_super_klass->is_declared_atomic()) {
7050       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7051     }
7052 
7053     if (_super_klass->is_interface()) {
7054       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7055       Exceptions::fthrow(
7056         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7057         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7058         "class %s has interface %s as super class",
7059         _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7060         _super_klass->external_name()
7061       );
7062       return;
7063     }
7064 
7065     // Make sure super class is not final
7066     if (_super_klass->is_final()) {
7067       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(), "Cannot inherit from final class");
7068     }
7069 
7070     // For an inline class, only java/lang/Object or special abstract classes
7071     // are acceptable super classes.
7072     if (is_inline_type()) {
7073       const InstanceKlass* super_ik = _super_klass;
7074       if (super_ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
7075         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7076         Exceptions::fthrow(
7077           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7078           vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7079           "inline class %s has an invalid super class %s",
7080           _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7081           _super_klass->external_name());
7082         return;
7083       }
7084     }
7085   }
7086 
7087   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_NonTearable() && _loader_data->class_loader() == NULL) {
7088     // This is the original source of this condition.
7089     // It propagates by inheritance, as if testing "instanceof NonTearable".
7090     _is_declared_atomic = true;
7091   } else if (*ForceNonTearable != '\0') {
7092     // Allow a command line switch to force the same atomicity property:
7093     const char* class_name_str = _class_name->as_C_string();
7094     if (StringUtils::class_list_match(ForceNonTearable, class_name_str)) {
7095       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7096     }
7097   }
7098 
7099   // Set ik->invalid_inline_super field to TRUE if already marked as invalid,
7100   // if super is marked invalid, or if is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()
7101   // returns true
7102   if (invalid_inline_super() ||
7103       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->invalid_inline_super()) ||
7104       is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()) {
7105     set_invalid_inline_super();
7106   }
7107 
7108   if (!is_inline_type() && invalid_inline_super() && (_super_klass == NULL || !_super_klass->invalid_inline_super())
7109       && !_implements_identityObject && class_name() != vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
7110     _temp_local_interfaces->append(SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass());
7111     _has_injected_identityObject = true;
7112   }
7113   int itfs_len = _temp_local_interfaces->length();
7114   if (itfs_len == 0) {
7115     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
7116   } else if (itfs_len == 1 && _temp_local_interfaces->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
7117     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
7118   } else {
7119     _local_interfaces = MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(_loader_data, itfs_len, NULL, CHECK);
7120     for (int i = 0; i < itfs_len; i++) {
7121       _local_interfaces->at_put(i, _temp_local_interfaces->at(i));
7122     }
7123   }
7124   _temp_local_interfaces = NULL;
7125   assert(_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7126 
7127   // Compute the transitive list of all unique interfaces implemented by this class
7128   _transitive_interfaces =
7129     compute_transitive_interfaces(_super_klass,
7130                                   _local_interfaces,
7131                                   _loader_data,
7132                                   CHECK);
7133 
7134   assert(_transitive_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7135 
7136   // sort methods
7137   _method_ordering = sort_methods(_methods);
7138 
7139   _all_mirandas = new GrowableArray<Method*>(20);
7140 
7141   Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7142   klassVtable::compute_vtable_size_and_num_mirandas(&_vtable_size,
7143                                                     &_num_miranda_methods,
7144                                                     _all_mirandas,
7145                                                     _super_klass,
7146                                                     _methods,
7147                                                     _access_flags,
7148                                                     _major_version,
7149                                                     loader,
7150                                                     _class_name,
7151                                                     _local_interfaces,
7152                                                     CHECK);
7153 
7154   // Size of Java itable (in words)
7155   _itable_size = is_interface() ? 0 :
7156     klassItable::compute_itable_size(_transitive_interfaces);
7157 
7158   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
7159   assert(_parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
7160 
7161 
7162   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
7163     if (Signature::basic_type(fs.signature()) == T_VALUETYPE  && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
7164       // Pre-load value class
7165       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::resolve_inline_field_or_fail(&fs,
7166           Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
7167           _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
7168       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
7169       assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Value type expected");

7170     }
7171   }
7172 
7173   _field_info = new FieldLayoutInfo();
7174   if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
7175     FieldLayoutBuilder lb(class_name(), super_klass(), _cp, _fields,
7176         _parsed_annotations->is_contended(), is_inline_type(),
7177         loader_data(), _protection_domain, _field_info);
7178     lb.build_layout(CHECK);
7179     if (is_inline_type()) {
7180       _alignment = lb.get_alignment();
7181       _first_field_offset = lb.get_first_field_offset();
7182       _exact_size_in_bytes = lb.get_exact_size_in_byte();
7183     }
7184   } else {
7185     layout_fields(cp, _fac, _parsed_annotations, _field_info, CHECK);
7186   }
7187   _has_inline_fields = _field_info->_has_inline_fields;
7188 
7189   // Compute reference type
7190   _rt = (NULL ==_super_klass) ? REF_NONE : _super_klass->reference_type();
7191 }
7192 
7193 void ClassFileParser::set_klass(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7194 
7195 #ifdef ASSERT
7196   if (klass != NULL) {
7197     assert(NULL == _klass, "leaking?");
7198   }
7199 #endif
7200 
7201   _klass = klass;
7202 }
7203 
7204 void ClassFileParser::set_klass_to_deallocate(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7205 
7206 #ifdef ASSERT
7207   if (klass != NULL) {
7208     assert(NULL == _klass_to_deallocate, "leaking?");
7209   }
7210 #endif
7211 
7212   _klass_to_deallocate = klass;
7213 }
7214 
7215 // Caller responsible for ResourceMark
7216 // clone stream with rewound position
7217 const ClassFileStream* ClassFileParser::clone_stream() const {
7218   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
7219 
7220   return _stream->clone();
7221 }

7223 // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
7224 // debugging
7225 
7226 #ifdef ASSERT
7227 
7228 // return true if class_name contains no '.' (internal format is '/')
7229 bool ClassFileParser::is_internal_format(Symbol* class_name) {
7230   if (class_name != NULL) {
7231     ResourceMark rm;
7232     char* name = class_name->as_C_string();
7233     return strchr(name, JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT) == NULL;
7234   } else {
7235     return true;
7236   }
7237 }

7239 #endif
